Xinjiang Diplomatic Envoy Wu Aichen Meets with Luo Wengan

(Nanjing) Wu Jingchen, Xinjiang Diplomatic Envoy, departed from Moscow on March 7th and arrived in Beijing on the night of the 4th. He reported to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs on the 5th, awaiting an audience with President Wang Jingwei. He met with Minister Luo of the Ministry of Judicial Administration on the 5th. According to the discussion: (1) The Sheng-Ma conflict has indeed come to an end. Ma has led his troops deep into southern Xinjiang from Turpan. The disaster of war has not been extinguished, and there is a risk of recurrence in the future. (2) Zhang Peiyuan was indeed killed in a sniper attack during the loss of the army. (3) The independent situation in southern Xinjiang has become a reality. When Minister Luo toured Xinjiang last year, he originally intended to go to southern Xinjiang to offer comfort, and the people were prepared to warmly welcome him. However, due to the resumption of the Sheng-Ma war and the obstruction of transportation, Luo did not go, resulting in today's situation, which is deeply regrettable. The current independent situation is only manipulated by a few leaders, and the people still oppose it. If a solution is found as soon as possible, it can still be saved. (4) The overall situation in Xinjiang is extremely complex, especially in terms of diplomacy. Various countries are manipulating and instigating. If we do not fully respond, the destruction is worrisome. (5) I have been in Xinjiang for many years. I was summoned back to Beijing and will present all the details I know for your reference. (Central News Agency dispatch from the 5th)

Japanese Activities in Europe (Continued) World Telegraph Service

Economic and Political Advance Threatens All Countries

Using Money to Make Unfavorable Propaganda Against Our Country

The situation in Ethiopia is such, and the situations in other places on both sides of the Red Sea, such as Egypt, Syria, and Iraq, are also largely the same. Egypt was originally a market that the British were confident they could monopolize for a long time through political power, but because of the devaluation of the Japanese currency, the extremely low Japanese wages, and the fact that Japanese women and children also work day and night with men, the price of Japanese goods is extremely low, and British goods cannot compete no matter what. In ten years, Japan's exports to Egypt have jumped from 558,000 pounds to 2,152,000 pounds. On the other hand, the trade of the British in the Nile region, taking only textiles produced in Lanka City as an example, has decreased by half in sales.

The above describes the Japanese economic activities in Europe. Whether in Europe or in places outside Europe that Europeans have always regarded as economic spheres of influence, it is, in short, a threat that Europeans have gradually and deeply felt since the September 18th Incident. Before the September 18th Incident, Europeans believed that Japan's military power was inviolable, and that Japan's position in East Asia was something they could do nothing about. After the September 18th Incident, after many new facts, they further felt that Japan was terrible, not only in the Pacific. Japan's aggression does not only rely on military strength. In today's Europe and the United States, where all industries are depressed, there are still Japanese people coming to seize the European market on which they depend for survival. This cannot help but make them wary and recall the phantom of the "Yellow Peril."

In addition to economic activities, let's take a look at political activities. Since Japan withdrew from the League of Nations, Japan seems to have no political activities in Europe on the surface. In fact, it is not the case. When the September 18th Incident occurred, Europe and the United States were in the midst of an economic panic. Neither the United States, Russia, nor the major powers had the strength to intervene in the dramatic changes in the Far East. These countries knew that the current Japan was taking advantage of the chaos to fish in troubled waters. If you don't have the real power to subdue him, then he will not give up. Therefore, instead of acting impulsively and rashly breaking with him, it is better to endure for a while and wait until the difficulties of the countries themselves are resolved before planning a comprehensive response. Japan also saw through this trick, so after seizing the four northeastern provinces, it temporarily stopped further aggression and first devoted all its efforts to managing and enriching the land it had already obtained in order to consolidate its foundation on the mainland. This can be naturally understood by looking at the recent actions of Japan in the Northeast. On the one hand, they never stop military rectification. The strength of the Japanese navy has already exceeded the 5:5:3 ratio compared to the United Kingdom and the United States, because although the number of ships and tonnage of Japan on the surface meet the 5:5:3 ratio, in fact, Japan is building many warships there in the name of other countries (such as South American countries). Once something happens, the shipbuilders will not deliver the ships to the original owners, and those many warships will all become Japan's own warships. The navy is like this, and the army and air force are also constantly expanding there. At the same time, Puyi's usurpation is naturally a profound warning from Japan to China and the world. Although the resumption of diplomatic relations between the United States and Russia is somewhat enough to add to the concerns of the Japanese, the Japanese know that the United States and Russia are difficult to win, and the Japanese also know that the United States and Russia are tolerant and self-respecting and will not easily try. What Japan is planning is not now but in the future.

What Japan fears in the future is (1) the joint actions of the United States, the United Kingdom, and Russia, which have interests in China and the Pacific, against Japan, and (2) the revival of China. Anyone with historical knowledge who understands the world situation has no doubt about the latter. Although the slowness is difficult to predict, the former may not come true because of the latter. Conversely, the more time the latter takes, the more inevitable the former becomes. Mussolini's so-called [The fate of the Pacific depends on the role played by the Chinese in this century] is most meaningful if interpreted in this way. In short, Japan's activities in Europe are completely centered on these two ideas, that is, on the one hand, using Germany and France to contain the United Kingdom, Russia, and the United States, so that they have no time to take care of themselves, and on the other hand, trying to cover up his conspiracy to provoke discord in China and seek to prolong China's chaos and disunity. It also uses the news agencies that take retainers of international news agencies and its own propaganda to make Europeans disappointed in China and to make China's international position increasingly degenerate.

The ingenuity and flexibility of Japan's propaganda business are truly admirable. The expenses paid by the Japanese government and the financial community for this business are not within the reach of our current strength. There is no message from the Japanese Associated Press that is not published. If the place of the dispatch is only Japan, only the Northeast estimated by Japan, it is not surprising. The wonderful thing is that there are often messages stating that they are from Nanjing, Shanghai, Beiping, or Guangzhou, so it should be messages from the Chinese side, but they often say things that are unfounded, fabricated, to deceive European readers, and to slander China. For example, saying that so-and-so is pro-Japanese, that a certain important person advocates Sino-Japanese cooperation, or that a certain general and a certain general are fighting again, or that the Communist Party is approaching a certain place, that bandits are rampant in a certain place, or that a certain border area is independent. Of these messages, one out of ten is often close to the truth, and the messages that are unfavorable to China are always the same, because there are people like Chong Deqiu Shui who are stationed in Europe all the time and are proficient in the European news business, because there is also money, so these messages are sent, not only are they not published, but they are also said to be from Nanjing when they are published, the newspaper says they are from Nanjing, and they are said to be from Guangzhou, the newspaper says they are from Guangzhou. Anyway, the Chinese messages that the Japanese provide to European newspapers, the Chinese themselves are still dreaming. A drop of water can become a river. Such bad news is often published in European newspapers and magazines. I ask, can people who only rely on newspapers to get knowledge have a good impression of China? It is a pity that China only had a news agency in Europe after the September 18th Incident. The days are still short and the capital is limited. However, fortunately, there is this news agency. Europeans are gradually getting real Chinese news from the Chinese. Just in the past short period of time, the contribution of this news agency can be said to be very valuable. However, in order to be on par with the Japanese Associated Press, there must be strong capital, there must be government rewards, and there must be practical and long-term assistance from the business community.

This is to say that the Japanese are using propaganda in Europe to deceive the facts and damage China. As for Japan's desire to use Germany and France to contain the United Kingdom, Russia, and the United States, this is also an obvious fact. Germany and Japan are both countries that have withdrawn from the League of Nations. Since Hitler came to power, Germany and Russia have been incompatible. If Russia has something to do in the Far East, it is inevitable that there will be worries in Western Europe. When the relationship between Japan and Russia was dangerous, some people spread the rumor that Germany and Japan had newly established a kind of understanding. France has no interests in the Far East, but the French right-wing party feels that if the United Kingdom, the United States, and Russia have disputes with Japan in the Pacific, France's position in Europe will not be shaken. France's diplomacy is very simple, and it does not have to worry about the unpredictable changes in the attitude of the United Kingdom all the time, and it does not have to feel the pressure of Soviet Russian communists, and it is not often left and right by the economic and diplomatic power of the United States. Japan also has a secret calculation for France, which is to absorb huge French capital into Manchuria. In the future, this capital may get the same result as the capital that France lent to Imperial Russia, in other words, it will be turned into nothing. But at least the Japanese can use this capital to develop the Northeast in front of them, and at the same time, they can use France in the Northeast to contain Russia and the United States. This wishful thinking unfortunately has some common interests with what the French right-wing party thinks, so after the September 18th Incident, when the French right-wing cabinet was in power, Japan secretly tried its best to propose a Franco-Japanese alliance, and also tried to persuade the French to establish a loan of one million francs, but both of them were not approved by the French left-wing party, so there was no result in the end. Recently, the French radical socialist party has lost power, and soon there will be news that the plan of a Franco-Japanese joint banking group to operate in Manchurian industries is about to be realized. We hope that this is just a remnant of the failure of Japan's large-scale loan to France, and we hope that French right-wing politicians will not fall into the trap of Japanese cunning. (March 14th in Paris)

Japanese Plan to Invade North China

Reconnaissance and Surveying Begin to Take Action

Ultimate Goal to Occupy Tacheng

Troop Deployments Being Adjusted

Beijing News. The situation in North China has become increasingly dangerous. In fact, no one knows the specific details of the Japanese invasion policy and steps. According to the Mainland News Agency, they are recorded as follows:

Invasion Policy

The Japanese divide their policy of invading North China into three steps: first, destroying the important places in North China, and second, deploying an encirclement.

Important News from the Tangshan Labor Strike Regarding the Construction Industry

Qixin Magnetic Factory in Tangshan has been selling various jars and bricks in Shanghai for many years, especially the 6-inch square red ones, which are the most popular. However, since the beginning of this year, labor strikes have been occurring frequently in Tangshan and other parts of North China, causing transportation difficulties. The strikes have become particularly severe in recent days, and it is feared that they will not be resolved in the short term. The existing stock of various jars and bricks in Shanghai is limited. In addition to urgently telegraphing Tangshan to immediately ship all manufactured goods to Shanghai to meet the urgent needs, we are also publishing this announcement to the construction and building industries, urging them to quickly come to negotiate to avoid delaying their projects.

General Manager: Hengda Foreign Company, Qixin Magnetic Factory Shanghai Office.

Address: 1st Floor, Hamilton Building, Jiangxi Road. Telephone: 13544

Third, increasing latent forces: The first step has passed, namely the end of the battles at the various passes of the Great Wall. The second step is the increase of Japanese troops in the Malanyu and eastern Chahar's second and fourth districts. The third step is the expansion, organization, and supply of bandits in eastern Rehe and eastern Chahar, as well as the liaison between bandits in Hebei and Chahar provinces. Both steps have been gradually completed. Former intelligence personnel have now been ordered to cease activities, and the 1 million yuan monthly fund for intelligence activities by the Japanese embassy in North China has been abolished. An International Military Intelligence Department has been established. It is said that the fixed location of this department is in Tianjin, or some say in Peiping. It is divided into male and female groups. It is said that the leader of the male group is Tadatsugu Araki, and the leader of the female group is Yoshiko Kawashima. It is still impossible to find out who holds the position of the minister. In addition to the intelligence department, there is also a surveying and mapping agency, which seems to be directly under the jurisdiction of the Japanese garrison. The surveying and mapping work began in the winter of last year. The first surveying and mapping target was the Yellow River. The section from Luoyang to Kaifeng has been completed. The contents include: (1) the width of the river, (2) the depth of the riverbed, (3) the defensive terrain on both banks, (4) which section is suitable for crossing the river, and (5) an investigation of the current ships. The second surveying and mapping target is the route connecting Chahar-Mongolia and Xinjiang, and the shortcut connecting Suiyuan and Xinjiang. This work is currently underway. More than 20 radio stations have been set up from Rehe to western Mongolia, and short-wave radio stations are gradually increasing as the surveying and mapping team moves forward.

Current Objective

Although Japan is now actively making intimidating gestures of aggression towards North China, it is not actually in a hurry to encompass North China. This is probably the established policy of the Japanese military. However, recently, soldiers at home and abroad have been divided into two factions with different opinions. The domestic faction focuses on Russia and is unwilling to take any action until war is declared with Russia. The foreign faction is afraid that the time will be too late, creating an opportunity for military liaison between China and Russia. Therefore, they advocate establishing a second puppet regime in North China to divide China's internal strength, as well as political and military control in North China. It is still impossible to know which faction will ultimately prevail. There are rumors that Japan will help the puppet regime invade Peiping to build a fake capital, but this is purely speculation. Japan only has room to exploit the puppet regime and has no possibility of assisting it. It is clear that Japan does not want the puppet regime to gain strength. Therefore, its current objective, if the foreign military faction wins, is to establish a second puppet regime in North China; if the domestic military faction wins, it will temporarily abandon its ambition to invade and occupy North China.

Future Intentions

The actual purpose of Japan's current active westward advance is to occupy Tacheng in Xinjiang. It does not seem to have any plans for Chahar yet, but it is not without this ambition, just that the time is not ripe. Its intention to occupy Tacheng is to prevent the liaison between the extreme land forces of Soviet Russia on the one hand and to cut off the communication route between China and the Soviet Union on the other, avoiding the great taboo of being attacked from both sides. According to reliable information obtained by foreigners, the Japanese are preparing to achieve their goal over a period of one year. Various military deployments are also being coordinated, fully adopting a new organizational structure. Tank units and chemical warfare units are the backbone of the entire army, and cavalry will account for six-tenths of the main force. It is expected that the completion of this plan will be the time when the Russo-Japanese War breaks out. The current talk of a Russo-Japanese war is still far off.

Legends of the Dalai Lama's Resurrection After Death

| A Retrospective on the Dalai Lama's Death and the Events Surrounding It |

The *North China Daily News* reports that the 50 lamas sent by the Tibetan government to Nanjing to request the return of the Panchen Lama to Tibet boarded a ship in the Bay of Bengal yesterday to come to China. Meanwhile, a legend of the Dalai Lama's resurrection after death has suddenly arisen in the Kalimpong area. Although its truth or falsehood is yet to be determined, it is quite interesting. It is recorded below:

About a week before the Dalai Lama's death, the former abbot of Gaden Monastery went to Potala Palace to visit the Dalai Lama but was prevented by Gong Xierla, the Dalai Lama's trusted servant. At that time, the Dalai Lama was already suffering from a serious illness. Gong Xierla then informed the masses of a certain person who was believed to be possessed by the spirit of the god who protects Tibet and Buddhism. This person had been formally appointed by the Tibetan government to guide national affairs, both public and private. The medicine that Gong Xierla administered to the Dalai Lama was prescribed by this person. Unexpectedly, after taking the medicine, the Dalai Lama's condition worsened. By December 16th, he was barely breathing. The former abbot of Gaden Monastery was summoned early in the morning, but by the time he arrived, the Dalai Lama had already left this world. Thereupon, the man recited prayers several times and prayed for the Dalai Lama's resurrection. Remarkably, the Dalai Lama actually regained consciousness and said in a faint voice to the former abbot that he should summon the prime minister and four key cabinet members. The prime minister was the Dalai Lama's nephew. It is believed that the Dalai Lama informed the former abbot about his reincarnation and instructed the prime minister on the handling of state affairs in his will. However, this conversation was extremely private, and no one knew about it except for those nearby attendants. It is said that after the Dalai Lama finished instructing, he ate a small amount of food. Shortly thereafter, he closed his eyes again and passed away in front of the prime minister and cabinet members. The next day, December 18th, a seven-week mourning period was officially announced, and singing and dancing were prohibited. All civilians were required to wear white, women were not allowed to wear jewelry, shops were closed, and all flags and banners were taken down. However, three weeks later, the aforementioned proclamation was rescinded. Shortly thereafter, the authorities ordered the arrest of Gong Xierla and three of his relatives. Upon hearing the news, his father fled in disguise with 50,000 rupees but was eventually arrested in Darjeeling and brought back to Lhasa for imprisonment. Gong Xierla was interrogated, and then the person possessed by the spirit was arrested and punished for prescribing the medicine improperly. However, the person attributed it to the mischief of the evil spirit Niyetrul and was spared further investigation. Niyetrul was a learned lama who was known for his loyalty to the central government during his lifetime. When the Tibetan troops invaded the east, he was imprisoned in Darjeeling and committed suicide out of resentment. Before dying, he said that he would make the Dalai Lama uneasy in his position after becoming a ghost because the Dalai Lama had ordered his imprisonment. Gong Xierla was also spared prosecution, but he was sentenced to life imprisonment in a certain temple for concealing the Dalai Lama's illness. His property was confiscated by the Tibetan government. A certain person in charge of the Lhatreng Monastery, aged twenty-three, was promoted to regent on February 15th of this year, in accordance with tradition. The procedure is as follows: the surnames of several candidates for regent are written on paper, sealed in wax balls, and placed in a golden cup, covered with silk. A religious ceremony is performed in front of a certain deity. Then, the silk is removed, and the wax balls are poured onto a table in front of the deity. The one that is closest to the deity is selected. If several balls are the same distance away, the one on the right is selected. It is said that the entire Tibetan people have great love and respect for the regent. The Dalai Lama also greatly respected him during his lifetime. It is said that the man possesses magical powers. Recently, there have been rumors that the Dalai Lama has been reincarnated in a certain place, but this statement is actually incorrect.

Huang Fu Leaves Peiping to Go South

First Visit Chiang in Jiangxi, Then Meet Wang in Nanjing

Political Affairs Handled by Chief Secretary He Qigong

Peiping Correspondence: Huang Fu, Chairman of the Political Reorganization Committee, departed from Peiping West Station at 5:30 p.m. today (3rd) for Hankou. Accompanying him were Advisor Ge Jingyou, Secretary He Jiecai, Assistant Secretary Wang Dagang, staff member Gao Renjian, and several guards. Mrs. Huang is scheduled to take the Peiping-Shanghai train to Shanghai on the 4th. It is said that Huang plans to return to Peiping in two months. The special train will arrive in Hankou at 3:00 a.m. on the 5th to meet with Zhang Xueliang and Zhang Qun. He will then take a warship to Jiujiang and transfer to the Nanxun Road to Nanchang to visit Chairman Chiang Kai-shek. He will then go to Nanjing to pay respects to Chairman Lin and meet with President Wang Jingwei. After that, he will go to Shanghai and spend a considerable period of time there before returning to Mogan Mountain for a visit, and then return to Peiping. After Huang leaves Peiping, the routine affairs of the Political Reorganization Committee will still be handled by Chief Secretary He Qigong. As for Huang's mission to the south, it is nothing more than discussing diplomacy with Japan and seeking stability in North China.

Huang's special train was prepared by the Peining Railway Bureau two weeks ago and parked at the East Station. It consisted of one covered freight car, one first-class compartment car, one first-class lounge car, one third-class sleeper car, one passenger car, and one guard car. At 1:00 p.m. today, it was ordered to move from the station to Fengtai. Then, it was ordered to switch tracks to the Peiping-Hankou Line and arrive at the West Station via Guang'anmen and the West Gate for standby. At 4:30 p.m., he went to the West Station. Those who saw him off included Gao Shengyue, representing He Yingqin, Mayor of Peiping Yuan Liang, Police Chief Yu Jinhe, and more than 50 other people. Huang arrived at the West Station by car at 5:15 p.m. After boarding the train, the special train departed. When Huang arrived at the station, the security was very tight, with soldiers and police densely deployed.

Huang's trip to the south was extremely secretive. At 2:00 p.m. today, Huang had already left the Diplomatic Building and first went to Jurentang to visit He Yingqin to bid farewell. At 3:00 p.m., he went to Xishengping Garden to bathe and temporarily invited Peiping Mayor Yuan Liang by telephone for a conversation. He then took a car to the station and boarded the No. 264 flower car. He summoned Yuan Liang and Shen Yi for a private conversation. When reporters also presented their cards requesting to see him, Huang, standing at the car door, said that he was going south for about five or six weeks, first to Nanchang to visit Chairman Chiang Kai-shek, and then to Nanjing to visit President Wang. After finishing his business, he would return to his ancestral home in Zhejiang to sweep the tombs. According to Secretary-General He Qigong, Huang will first go to Hankou, then to Nanchang to visit Chiang, and then to Nanjing to meet with President Wang to report on the political and diplomatic situation in North China. He will then return to his hometown in Mogan Mountain to sweep the tombs and will not be able to return to Peiping for about forty days. He only telegraphed the Executive Yuan in advance to report and did not ask for leave (3rd).

Chiang Issues General Order to Ten Provinces to Rectify Officialdom

Those Who Violate the Law Should Be Severely Punished

Do Not Lightly Dismiss Them

Nanchang Correspondence: The Nanchang Headquarters has recently issued a general order to the governments of Jiangsu, Zhejiang, Fujian, Henan, Hubei, Anhui, Hunan, Jiangxi, Shaanxi, and Gansu provinces to rectify officialdom. The original order states [Now that the country is facing a serious national crisis, after the careful selection and appointment of administrative officials at all levels, they should be granted a longer term of office and strict responsibilities so that they can gradually implement all important policies without the mindset of a five-day magistrate. For incidents that warrant punishment, they should be given reprimands, demerits, salary deductions, and demotions, depending on the severity of the circumstances. They should not be lightly dismissed, lest cunning people take advantage of minor offenses to evade their responsibilities. If there is serious illegal behavior, they should be imprisoned or executed accordingly, and should not be dismissed lightly to comply with the ancient principle of using heavy penalties in times of disorder. This is the most effective method to curb corruption and negligence and to protect the virtuous and capable. The key to clarifying officialdom and increasing efficiency lies entirely in this. At this time, when the declining trend is prevalent and the country is facing a serious crisis, it is especially necessary to rigorously implement the aforementioned various punishments and not to lightly dismiss them, otherwise it will be impossible to revive the country. I hope that the administrative heads of each province and party will deeply understand this meaning and conscientiously implement it. In addition to issuing separate orders, I hereby order the provincial governments to comply and instruct their subordinates to be informed. This order is issued by Chairman Chiang Kai-shek] (April 4th)

Liu's Bandits Flee Into Jiangsu Province

Ganyu County Seat Has Been Occupied

Wang Jun Dispatches Troops to Encircle and Suppress

Xuzhou Correspondence: After Liu Guitang's bandit gang fled back into Shandong province, they were attacked by Sun Tongxuan, Gu Liangmin, and other troops dispatched by Han Fuju. The bandits, having been on the run for a long time and exhausted, would collapse without a fight when faced with a large-scale military suppression. However, the bandits were mostly natives of eastern Shandong, familiar with the geography, and their movements were extremely unpredictable. They have recently fled south from Yishui into Jiangsu. The Jinpu Garrison Command received a telegram from Han Fuju reporting this. Wang Jun immediately dispatched the 19th Brigade, led by Li Shilong, stationed in Xuzhou, to take two trains east yesterday morning to defend the Xin'an Town area. Then, he received news that Liu's bandits had fled into Ganyu, a county under the jurisdiction of Hai Prefecture. Wang Jun again dispatched the 21st Brigade, led by Li Wenbin, stationed in Bengbu, to take two trains east last night to assist in the defense. In the evening, news came from the front that about 800 of Liu's bandits had surrounded Ganyu County Seat. Wang Jun immediately ordered Li Shilong's troops to advance rapidly towards Qingkou from the Caopu and Baitabu stations. This morning (4th), news was received that the bandits had captured Ganyu County Seat. Wang then led the chief of the staff section Su Ziwen, aide-de-camp Zhou Chuanduo, and telegraph operators and guards to the east on a special train at 12:00 noon to supervise the suppression between Xin'an and Xinpu. Ganyu is located in the northernmost part of the four counties under the jurisdiction of Hai Prefecture, adjacent to Shandong province. Qingkou is south of Ganyu County Seat, and Xinpu is south of Qingkou. After the bandits entered Ganyu County Seat, major stores and financial institutions in Qingkou moved their important items to Xinpu. The 7th Division troops were deployed north of the Longhai Line, and armored trains patrolled between Xuzhou and Haizhou. Before departing, Wang Jun told reporters at the station, "Li's brigade will be able to pass Qingkou this afternoon. If Liu's bandits stay in the city, they will definitely be surrounded and resolved. However, the bandits' intention is to loot money, not to occupy the land. I am afraid that once our troops arrive, they will flee again. I have telegraphed Han and Fang to ask them to dispatch troops to track and pursue. The Shandong army will attack from north to south, and our army will attack from south to north. The two sides will attack from both sides, and they will definitely be annihilated. It is heard that the Shandong army is deployed on the Shandong border, and it is not easy for the bandits to flee back. They will inevitably flow into Jiangsu province. Therefore, in addition to sending a part of the army to Ganyu this year, we will still pay attention to the interception of bandits flowing along the Longhai Line to prevent the bandits from crossing the line and causing serious trouble to the local area." Dong Yaotang, director of the Longhai Road Office in Xuzhou, also took a car to Xin'an this morning to facilitate the coordination of train and military transportation. As for the bandits entering Ganyu County Seat, they have looted extensively. As of this evening, there is no news of their withdrawal. The extent of the losses and whether there are any kidnappings are not yet known. There are not many garrison troops in Hai Prefecture, and local police forces are all guarding their respective areas. Tongshan and the counties east of Xuzhou have also dispatched police teams to defend the borders, coupled with the suppression by the large army, the bandits may not cross the line and flee south. (4th)

Songjiang

The Ministry of Justice Sends Personnel to Inspect Prison Administration

The Ministry of Judicial Administration is organizing the national prisons, first conducting inspections to provide a basis for improvement. Zhou Zhenzuo, a technician from the ministry, and Wang Yuanzeng, director of the Prison Department, arrived in Songjiang today to inspect the equipment of the court prison and detention center. At noon, County Magistrate Jin hosted a banquet at the county government to welcome them and inquired in detail about the judicial situation in the county. It is heard that Zhou and Wang will leave for Jinshan and other counties tomorrow for inspection. After completing their work, they will return to the capital to report.

The Seventh Aunt of Baolian is Re-coffined

Shi Tao Hai, the son of the manager of the Songjiang Salt Office, redeemed the body of Baolian's seventh aunt from the Shanghai Xiaohua Garden brothel and married her as a concubine, hiding her in a golden house. However, just three days later, a tragic murder occurred. After the procuratorate verified the cause of death, it ordered the undertaker to prepare a coffin and collect the body. Later, the pimp learned of this and notified the deceased's family in Yixing. Yesterday, together with the seventh aunt's sister, they filed a lawsuit with the court to claim the coffin and belongings. The seventh aunt's sister felt that the coffining was inadequate. The pimp also cried sadly and negotiated with the Shi family to transport the coffin to the Haoyuan Cemetery, purchase a top-grade coffin and burial clothes, and re-coffin the body, spending about 300 yuan. The body is temporarily placed in the cemetery for selection of a burial site.

Suzhou

Large Quantities of Narcotics Seized at the Station

The stationmaster of the Suzhou station on the Jinpu Railway seized four large boxes of raw materials for making narcotic pills, weighing over 500 catties, from passengers Jiang Jingsheng and Jin Zhiyuan on a passenger train from Shanghai on the 31st of last month. It is said that they were sent to the Renji Pharmacy in Suzhou City for receipt. The raw materials were sent to the Fuyin Hospital outside the Qimen gate for testing, and the passengers were detained at the station. However, because the Fuyin Hospital did not have a testing room, the original items were returned to the station. This matter was discovered by Liu Hong, a patrol officer of the third section of the Suzhou station police. He took the raw materials for the narcotic pills and the two passengers to the police station and reported to the police departments and management bureaus of both railways. Yesterday (5th), a reply telegram was received ordering the transfer of the raw materials to Shanghai for testing.

A Traveler Commits Suicide in the Su Tai Inn

A traveler named Wang Huiyu, a native of Ningbo, aged 27, came to the Lao Su Tai Inn outside the gate on the 27th of last month with his wife Liu Caiyun, his five-year-old son, and a suitcase. He booked room No. 50. On the 30th, he moved to room No. 28. The day before yesterday (4th), the couple took their son out in the afternoon. At 4:00 p.m., Wang Huiyu returned to the inn alone before his wife. At 6:00 p.m., Liu and her son returned and found the door locked. They shouted and knocked loudly. After a long time, a voice inside responded and opened the door. The waiter Wu Yongshan knew something was wrong and went inside to investigate. He found a bottle of Anshe medicine and two letters beside the pillow, indicating that he had taken poison. He immediately reported to the police officer and sent him to the Suyong Hospital for treatment. He is currently conscious. His family is still staying at the inn. When a reporter visited him yesterday morning, Wang refused to speak. However, it is known that Wang lived in Hongkou, Shanghai, and worked at the Gold and Silver Exchange. Due to business failure and difficult living conditions, he came to Suzhou to ask his brother-in-law (currently a military supply officer in the 88th Division) for help but failed. Therefore, he committed suicide.

Wuxi

Second Labor Strike Occurs at Qingfeng

The Qingfeng Yarn Factory in Zhoushan浜, due to improving work efficiency, replaced the male workers in the original steel-wire station with female workers. The laid-off male workers were reassigned to miscellaneous jobs. The workers expressed their dissatisfaction, causing a huge strike on the 21st of last month. After the party and government summoned all relevant parties and negotiated eight principles for mediation, the workers resumed work first, and then elected Xu Yongji, Yang Hanxi, Cheng Jingtang, and Chen Xiangchun to be responsible for the review in order to thoroughly resolve the issue. The county government sent a letter to each reviewer, scheduling a meeting for the review. Unexpectedly, the female workers in the weaving machine room had a conflict over the issue of fines at 3:00 p.m. the day before yesterday (4th), resulting in the destruction of the cloth inspection platform and windows in the cloth inspection room, and the books of fines were also torn up. Tang Guizhen and Zhu Huifen, female workers in the cloth inspection room, and Yang Zhemin, a male worker, were slightly injured. Wang Zhizhi, an employee of the cloth inspection room, was also hit by a copper pipe by the workers. At that time, the order was chaotic. After 6:00 p.m., more than 290 female workers in the weaving machine room all left the factory gate. Then, they gathered to discuss the matter. Yesterday, they brought along the spinning workers and also stopped working. Tang Xinghai, the factory director, immediately reported the situation to the county government and requested assistance in maintaining order. The workers, represented by female worker leaders Xu Axiu, Xu Lindi, Ge Aiyuan, Wang Xiaomei, Fan Xiaoying, and Zheng Qiaoyun, also reported to the county government through the labor union, claiming that the workers would be willing to have their wages deducted if their work was inferior. However, they should not be held responsible for issues such as yellow water, black spots, and uneven thickness, loose weave, etc., or if there was coal ash in the factory, or if the raw materials were not good, or if the machinery was too old. They proposed three conditions: (1) unanimously oppose female cloth inspectors, (2) refuse a certain employee of the cloth inspection room, Ding, to enter the factory again in the future, and (3) the reduction of wages should not exceed four points at most. The factory stated that, according to the cloth woven by female workers last year, 80 out of every 100 pieces could be considered A-grade (Double Fish), with only 20 pieces being considered B-grade (Cowherd). This year, only 40 out of every 100 pieces can be considered A-grade, with the rest having defects. Therefore, it is necessary to be more serious about the work. As for rewards, a total of 104 yuan and eight jiao in cloth weaving rewards and 332 yuan and one jiao and nine fen in material rewards were given in March. However, a strike still occurred, which is unfortunate. At 2:00 p.m. yesterday, the workers gathered at the labor union and then braved the rain to petition the county party headquarters and the county government, stating their difficulties in person. County Magistrate Yan received them and ordered them to resume work first and wait for a resolution after convening a meeting with the party headquarters.

Changzhou

Incestuous Relationship Between Aunt and Nephew-in-Law Causes Murder

A floating corpse was discovered in Dongqiaodi, Qinglian Township, the 16th District of Wuyi County, on the morning of the 5th. Wang Jun, the acting township head of the township, reported the incident to the district office, requesting that it be forwarded to the county prosecutor's office to send someone to conduct an autopsy. Zhou Weizhu and Zhou Weiyin from the township reported that their brother, Zhou Weisi, had suddenly disappeared. They requested Township Head Wang to accompany them to inspect the floating corpse. They saw that the deceased was indeed their brother, Weisi. Township Head Wang then inquired with the deceased's mother, Zhou Wei, who learned that the brothers had been arguing over property and that an incestuous relationship had occurred between her daughter-in-law and her nephew-in-law, resulting in Weisi being killed by Zhou Li and Zhou Ruilin. However, Zhou Li and Zhou Ruilin had already fled. Township Head Wang believed that the case involved murder and immediately dispatched the security team to investigate. They arrested the two in Qiuzhuang Village. He waited for Chief Prosecutor Yang Kongxi to come to the township for an autopsy. The autopsy confirmed that he had been strangled to death with a rope and thrown into the river. He ordered the family to collect the body and scheduled a hearing at the court on the 5th for all parties involved in the case. The criminals arrested by the security team were also sent to the court on the 5th for questioning.

Nantong

Conflict Between Militia and Farmers Causes Bloodshed

A conflict occurred between the security team of the Fifth District and farmers in Xiangjiaqiao over the collection of land donations. The team members opened fire, killing and injuring many men and women, inciting public outrage. Liu Jinshan, the team member who caused the incident, was arrested and sent to the court. After the prosecutor's investigation, he was prosecuted with the death penalty. The criminal court scheduled the trial for the 17th.

Local Court Scheduled to Be Established

In order to facilitate civil and criminal litigation for parties in counties such as Ruhai, Taizhou, and Jingjiang in northern Jiangsu, the Ministry of Judicial Administration has ordered the Nantong County Court to be upgraded and reorganized into a local court. Preparations are underway, and it is scheduled to be established on July 1st.

Haimen

Affair Leads to Wife's Murder

Liu Shizhen, the deputy head of Jibin Town in the Sixth District, who is over thirty years old, married Chen Jinrong's daughter through a matchmaker in the past. They were initially on good terms, but later Liu began an affair with Xu Degang's eldest daughter, Muying. This led to frequent quarrels between the couple. The day before yesterday (2nd), one of Liu's small boxes suddenly disappeared, containing photos of Liu and Muying together. Suspecting that Chen had stolen it, he beat Chen severely with a wooden stick three times, causing injuries all over her body and making her moan in pain. That night, he strangled Chen to death with a rope. The next day, he hastily coffined and buried her to cover up the traces. The wife's family was weak and kind, and had not yet reported the case.

The High Court Sends Personnel to Re-examine the Gong Xueqing Case

Gong Xueqing, the adopted daughter-in-law of Gu Falin in Shijia Town in the First District, suddenly died in February. The family of the deceased reported to the county for an autopsy. Deng, the trial judge, went to conduct the autopsy. The family of the deceased forcibly tried to force Deng to conclude that she had died from fatigue but failed. They surrounded and insulted Deng. Later, County Magistrate Zhang led the police to re-examine the body and found scars on her waist and back and rope marks on her neck. However, it remained to be proven whether she had been strangled. Last month, the county government arrested and questioned the main culprits, Gong Huangshi and Gong Hongyuan. Details of the case have been reported in this newspaper twice. Later, Gong Huangshi, the family of the deceased, submitted a request to the county government to forward to the High Court for a re-examination. Xuan Zhiming, a forensic official from the High Court, arrived in Haimen in February. Yesterday (3rd), he opened the coffin at the Doutian Temple in the county seat and city to conduct a re-examination. The re-examination found whip marks on the upper right back of the deceased, rope marks on the neck from the root of the right ear to the jaw, an abrasion on the chest, and cyanosis on both fingernails. He concluded that she had hanged herself after being injured. His reasons were: 1. The rope marks ran from the root of the right ear to the jaw, while there were no rope marks on the left side. This was because her feet were off the ground when she hanged herself, her head tilted to the right, and the center of gravity shifted to the right. 2. The fingernails were cyanotic, which was because the body was hanging down during the suicide, and the blood congealed there. After the examination, the coffin was handed over to the town security to guard, pending a final decision before burial.

Hangzhou

Great Fire in Yuanfu Lane

This morning (the 5th) around 2:00 AM, a fire broke out at the Fangzheng Tea House warehouse, number 20 Yuanfu Lane, Hangzhou, due to the stored lime getting wet. The fire quickly became intense and was extinguished after burning for an hour. Several thousand catties of stored tea leaves and the entire warehouse were destroyed, with losses estimated at over 30,000 yuan. Fortunately, the fire did not spread to neighboring houses due to the tall surrounding walls of the warehouse.

Hefei

Ban on "Upside-Down Seven" Opera Leads to Police Injury

Since the Spring Festival, "Upside-Down Seven" operas (i.e., lewd and local operas) have been widely performed in urban and rural areas of Hefei. Initially, they were performed secretly, but now they are blatantly setting up stages, hiring female performers, and attracting customers, almost emptying the streets. On the 31st, Wu Jiatang and others performed with hired female performers behind the Great King Temple in the east suburbs, attracting over ten thousand spectators. Wang Jifu, a patrol officer from the East Suburbs Public Security Bureau, deemed the opera detrimental to public order and banned its performance, but his orders were ignored. That evening, the opera was staged with even greater fanfare. Wang led police to the scene and arrested seven male performers, including Chen Gongyu, Wang Shihe, and He Daoming, along with their gongs, drums, costumes, etc. However, the opera organizer led a crowd to the scene, and they attacked the police officers Ge Shihai and Wu Yugui, injuring their heads and causing them to bleed profusely. A rifle was seized and broken, and a rifle bolt was lost. Three of the opera performers were taken away by the crowd. Patrol Officer Wang then sent Chen Gongyu, He Daoming, Dai Wenchuan, and Wang Shihe to the Public Security Section for interrogation and treatment, while the injured police officers were taken to Mengjiu Hospital for treatment. The Public Security Section has reported the case to the county government and plans to arrest the opera organizer for punishment.

Local News

Kong Xiangxi Arrives in Shanghai Yesterday Morning, Issues Written Statement

No Reports Received on Tense Situation in North China

Ban Hong Incident Due to Deliberate Provocation

Tax Revenue Increased Compared to Previous Years, No Foreign Debt Incurred

According to the Central News Agency, Kong Xiangxi, Vice President of the Executive Yuan and Minister of Finance, left Nanjing by overnight train at 11:00 PM the night before and arrived at Zhenru at 7:20 AM yesterday morning. He went directly to his private residence on West Aiham Road to rest. Reporters from various newspapers visited Kong at his private residence yesterday afternoon and were received. He issued a written statement, which is detailed below:

Situation in North China Remains Unchanged

(Question) Recently, there have been rumors that the situation in North China is tense, and that Chairman Huang Fu unexpectedly went south at this time, and that President Wang and ministers were said to be flying to Jiangxi. What is the truth? (Answer) There are frequent messengers traveling to and from North China. I have not received any emergency reports personally, and the situation is the same as before. As for the rumors, I heard that they were caused by the remarks of Commissioner Zhang Puquan. In reality, the whole world and the entire country are in an emergency situation. Commissioner Zhang's intention was probably to prevent the people of the country from having a five-minute heat and indulging in pleasure, so he shouted loudly to awaken the people of the country and strengthen their patriotic hearts. As for Chairman Huang's going south, it is to report on his work and there is no other reason. Chairman Huang is usually a responsible person. Outside rumors say that he abandoned his post and returned south due to the emergency in North China. This is definitely not the case. There is no emergency news in North China. If there were, Chairman Huang, being a responsible person, would never try to avoid danger. As for whether President Wang will fly to Jiangxi, I have not heard of it. In short, Chairman Chiang is a member of the Central Political Council, and the authorities naturally need to meet and discuss important central issues. During the period of suppression, he is not convenient to leave the army. When necessary, the authorities will go to Jiangxi to discuss matters in person, which is normal. Outsiders do not understand and make many speculations, which is unnecessary.

Ban Hong is a Misinformation of Ban Nong

(Question) Reports say that the Yunnan border is alarmed. What is the truth? (Answer) The rumored Ban Hong incident, as far as I know, is a mistake for Ban Nong. Ban Hong is our country's territory, while Ban Nong does not belong to our country. China and Britain have always had harmonious relations. Britain has always had the style of a great power and would not use force to invade our country's territory. The rumors are either based on misinformation and exaggerated, or someone is deliberately provoking and slandering Sino-British relations. I hope the people of the country will pay attention.

There is No Such Thing as Foreign Loans

(Question) There are rumors that a foreign banking group has lent a large sum of money to our country. What is the truth? (Answer) Borrowing foreign loans is a matter under the jurisdiction of the Ministry of Finance. As the Minister of Finance, I have never heard of this matter. However, I recently heard that our banking industry plans to organize a silver company to facilitate foreign investment in our country's construction projects in the future. This matter may be based on this misinformation. Examining the use of foreign capital to develop industry is originally advocated by the late Premier. I believe that borrowing money for construction should belong to a truly profitable production industry, which can be used to repay the principal and interest in the future, and not like the indiscriminate borrowing and abuse of the former Peking government, which has led to the inability to repay until now, increasing the burden on the people and damaging the country's reputation. Instead of borrowing money like this, it is better to save and tighten spending and not borrow money. As for national debt, I have long had the intention of reorganizing it, but we must seek a solution slowly and cannot rely on foreign loans. Seeing that the world economy is still in a depression, countries are raising debts and raising funds from their own people. The British and American governments even have proposals to prohibit other countries from borrowing in their countries. Under such circumstances, even if China intends to borrow foreign debt, foreigners may not be able to invest.

Tax Revenue Increased Compared to Previous Years

(Question) How is the financial situation recently? (Answer) The tax revenue has been very good recently and has increased compared to the previous month. When I took office as the Minister of Finance, I showed the people of the country the way to increase revenue and reduce expenditure. Recently, the outside world only knows about increasing revenue, but does not know about the actual situation. Now the military and political authorities are actively working hard on reducing expenditure, hoping to achieve the goal of balancing revenue and expenditure in the short term.

Southwest Cooperation Can Be Realized

(Question) Recently, there have been reports about the issue of cooperation between the central government and the southwest. What is the truth? (Answer) Recently, there have been frequent messengers between the central government and the Guangdong side. Now, the comrades in the southwest have realized the deepening of internal and external troubles and that only unity can save the country. Cooperation is expected to be realized. This is truly a blessing for the country, because those who talk about saving the country but cannot sacrifice their prejudices and only sing high tunes, forcing others to agree with me, will only harm and mislead the country. We will not wait for others to destroy us, but we will destroy ourselves.

Yunnan Association in Shanghai Telegraphs Request to Demarcate Borders

For the British Army Occupying Ban Hong

Please Request the Government to Protest Severely

Since the British occupied Ban Hong in Yunnan Province, the Yunnan Association in Shanghai has been extremely angry. They held a joint meeting of the executive and supervisory committees at the Association Hall on Baker Road at 3:00 PM yesterday. More than ten people including Zhang Yaozeng, Lu Zhiyi, Zhao Zhi, etc. attended. Zhang Yaozeng chaired the meeting and Zhao Zhi recorded it. First, the chairman reported on the important truth of the British army's invasion of Yunnan and the significance of holding the meeting. Then, Zhao Yunyan, who had been sent by the Yunnan Provincial Government to conduct an on-site inspection of the Yunnan-Burma border, attended the meeting and reported in detail on the causes and consequences of the Yunnan-Burma border negotiations. The meeting then decided to respond to the proposal of the Association in Beijing to unite with associations in various provinces and cities to protest together, and to telegraph the National Government and the Yunnan Provincial Government to lodge a serious protest with the British government, demarcate the borders, and strive to strengthen national defense in order to be prepared for emergencies. The original telegram is excerpted as follows: National Government and Yunnan Provincial Government: Since the British army occupied Ban Hong, it has been many days. Although the people of Yunnan have unanimously opposed it, the British have not shown any remorse. Such open aggression is related to the national territory. How can our government not severely stop it and deal with it carefully? The opinion of our association is that first, we should lodge a serious protest with the British government, order the British army to quickly withdraw to its original defense, and stop all construction work on bridges and roads, so that the Ban Hong area can completely restore its original state. Second, the British occupation of Ban Hong, although it has other intentions, the uncertain border is the cause of the disaster. We should take this opportunity to propose that the governments of the two countries each send senior officials to impartially survey the border, and measure one by one the places that were once regarded as disputed areas, so that there will be no ambiguity between this boundary and that boundary, so that disputes can be permanently prevented. Third, the Yunnan-Burma border is intertwined, and the national defense boundary cannot be ignored. The sage Yang Yiqing said that when there is nothing, we should be prepared for something, and when there is something, we should be calm as if there is nothing. These words are enough for people to follow today. We should ask the government to quickly rectify the border of Yunnan Province and strive to strengthen it, and not delay any longer, so that we can be prepared for emergencies. The above three points are related to safety and dare not be silent. The situation is urgent, and we hope for a decisive action. This is fortunate for Yunnan and fortunate for the country. Yunnan Association in Shanghai.

Ministry of Industry and Commerce Pays Attention to Fishery Companies

Treacherous Merchants Are Induced to Sell Inferior Goods

According to the Central News Agency, since the January 28th Incident, the fishery merchants in this city have automatically inspected inferior goods. However, recently, a certain country's nationals, seeing that this movement in our country is not as enthusiastic as in the past, have induced treacherous merchants to organize a fishery company in name, with Chinese people coming forward, but actually all controlled by nationals of that country, so that they can sell inferior goods. Chamber of Commerce Telegraphs Central Government Requesting Discussion of Cigarette Tax Rates

Forty Chinese Cigarette Factories Are on the Brink of Ruin

Livelihood of Hundreds of Thousands of Tobacco Farmers is Severed

Since the cigarette unified tax was changed to the new tax rate, Chinese cigarette factories have been greatly affected due to the unequal treatment of upper and lower cigarettes. After repeated meetings and discussions, they submitted a request to the Ministry of Finance to organize a committee to publicly discuss the matter, but this has not been implemented. Recently, because the factories can no longer bear the burden of this unfair tax rate, they sent a letter to the National Federation of Chambers of Commerce yesterday, requesting that it be forwarded to the central government ministries and departments to implement it as soon as possible. The original text of the letter is as follows: Nanjing National Government Executive Yuan, Legislative Yuan, Ministry of Finance, Ministry of Industry and Commerce, Tax Department: Recently, we received a joint letter from Shanghai Minzhong Cigarette Company and other forty cigarette companies, stating that the current cigarette taxes are unequal in terms of high and low tax rates, and requesting that the Legislative Yuan, Ministry of Finance, Ministry of Industry and Commerce, Tax Department, and Shanghai Cigarette Factory Industry Association each select members to publicly discuss revising the cigarette tax rates. The original text, except for the direct submission by the cigarette companies, is omitted here. The letter ends with the statement that after the Minzhong and other cigarette companies jointly submitted the request for revision, the Ministry of Finance and the Tax Department had previously issued a letter to the Shanghai Cigarette Factory Industry Association, which was forwarded to the members' meeting for discussion, and a decision was made to prepare a written opinion and reply to the Tax Department. However, a month has passed and no instructions have been received. The merchants can no longer endure the unequal tax rates and have jointly requested your association to unanimously request, etc. In view of this, we find that the current cigarette tax rates are light for upper cigarettes and heavy for lower cigarettes, and the high and low treatments are indeed unfair. Moreover, the tobacco leaves for upper cigarettes mostly come from overseas, and the operation is mostly done by foreign merchants. The tobacco leaves for lower cigarettes are mostly produced locally, and the operation is mostly done by Chinese people. If we follow the principle of protecting taxes, we should levy heavy taxes on upper cigarettes and light taxes on lower cigarettes. Even if we do not do this, we should treat them equally so that Chinese merchants and foreign merchants have the possibility of competition. According to what the merchants said, during the seven-tier system of cigarette tax, there were as many as 150 or 160 Chinese cigarette factories, and the annual sales of tobacco leaves in several counties such as Susong reached nearly 400,000 bags. Since the quota was changed to three tiers, and then from three tiers to two tiers, Chinese cigarette factories have gradually closed down. Today, there are only forty or fifty remaining. The sales of tobacco leaves in Susong and other counties have also gradually decreased, with annual sales of only about 100,000 bags. Since the implementation of the new two-tier system at the end of last year, cigarette merchants have been the first to bear the brunt, and these forty or fifty factories are also in danger. Tobacco farmers are also indirectly harmed and will be left to die. Moreover, if the previous seven-tier system is restored, tax revenue can be greatly increased, while with the current two-tier system, tax revenue is reduced. The statements are very detailed and are all facts. This is especially important for the national economy and people's livelihood and is not only about the interests of Chinese and foreign merchants. Our government should pay special attention to it. Based on the above, we have attached the letter and telegraphed it to your departments for review and approval. We earnestly request that the Legislative Yuan, Ministry of Finance, Ministry of Industry and Commerce, Tax Department, and Shanghai Cigarette Factory Industry Association each send representatives to organize a cigarette tax rate discussion committee to publicly discuss the matter, either restoring the seven-tier system or collecting taxes based on value, so as to be fair and benefit the people's livelihood. Attached are two documents. National Federation of Chambers of Commerce.

Yesterday, the Chinese Ratepayers' Association Sent Two Sets of Election Ballots

Commercial Group: 182 Ballots

Native-Place Group: 165 Ballots

The 13th election of the Chinese Ratepayers' Association of the International Settlement, for the Commercial and Native-Place groups, sent out election ballots at 2:00 PM yesterday. Representatives Present

Yesterday, the 13th election ballots were distributed, and the following representatives were present: Zhu Wenqi from the Municipal Chamber of Commerce, Mao Heyuan from the Ningbo Native-Place Association, Lin Kanghou from the Banking Association, Zhang Yichen from the Citizens' Federation, Wu Rulin from the Money Industry Association, Qian Youlan from the Shaoxing Seven Counties Native-Place Association, and Xu Jizi, Wang Hanliang, Hu Fengxiang, and other representatives, more than ten in total.

The 81 representatives then mutually elect the executive committee members of the Association and the Chinese directors and committee members of the Municipal Council to participate in various administrative matters. The Citizens' Group of this election has already been elected on March 27. The Commercial and Native-Place groups sent out election ballots yesterday and are scheduled to vote on April 9 and count the ballots on April 10. After the above representatives are elected, a date will be set for mutually electing the executive committee members and Chinese directors and committee members.

Investigation Report

The election report of the 13th group of the Association states: In the election of this group, 93 investigation forms were received from commercial groups, of which 4 forms only nominated 1 person. Therefore, there were a total of 182 people. The election roster is numbered 182, and 182 election ballots were issued, matching the above number. 86 investigation forms were received from native-place groups, of which 5 forms only nominated 1 person. Therefore, there were a total of 167 people. The draft number of the election roster is 167. However, after the roster was compiled, the Citizens' Federation of the First Special District was suddenly allowed to open the names and addresses of the branches as a basis. Because the 13th District Branch was not listed, the investigation form of the Association was returned. Therefore, there were only 165 people in total. The official number of the election roster is 165, and only 165 election ballots were issued. Joint statement, April 5, 23rd year of the Republic of China.

Statement from Property Owners

Last Year's Water Bill Ratio to Rent

Highest at Over 20%

Municipal Council's Information Is Inaccurate

According to the New Voice News Agency, the Municipal Council of the International Settlement issued a news item about water bills yesterday, stating that half of last year's water bills were slightly more than 7.5% of the rent, and half were slightly less than 7.5%. In order to clarify the facts, the reporter inquired with the relevant property owners and was told that this year's water bill has been implemented since April 1. Although it is said that the bill is collected at an 80% discount, since it has not been a month, the water value has not yet been paid. Therefore, whether it is cheaper or increased compared to last year is not yet known. As for the report that last year's water bill was between 7.5% of the rent, this is not accurate. Because in the past, when the water bill was included in the rent, it was paid at 7.5% of the rent. Later, the water company suffered heavy losses when paying 7.5%. It was changed to 10%. Later, due to the rising gold price, the water company changed to the current system (water meter system) in order to increase revenue. In the central area of the International Settlement, because the rent is high, after changing to the water meter system, the water bill is about 7.5% of the rent, and there is no loss. It is still cheaper to calculate at 10%, so there are fewer disputes. The Hongkou District is a labor area, and the rent is low. After changing to the water meter system, the water bill has increased sharply, exceeding 20% of the rent at the highest point, and usually between 15% of the rent. Therefore, disputes have occurred repeatedly. It is completely wrong to say that the water bill borne by ordinary people is within 7.5%. Moreover, there are resolutions from the Real Estate Association that can be checked when mediating disputes and cannot be ignored. The situation described today is not worth a smile from knowledgeable people.

Chen Gongbo Arrives in Shanghai

Chen Gongbo left Beijing by overnight express train yesterday and arrived in Shanghai this morning.

Social Bureau Sets Today to Mediate Customs Brokerage Labor Dispute

Workers Arrested, Union Rescues

Union Reports Causes of Labor Dispute

After the Customs Brokerage workers went on strike due to the Tianjin gang customs brokers destroying the cartage precedents, the Social Bureau immediately sent personnel to investigate in detail and summoned both labor and management, strictly ordering the Customs Brokerage Association to be responsible for issuing cartage according to the precedents. Today at 2:00 PM, the Customs Brokerage Union and the Customs Brokerage Association will be summoned again for mediation. At the same time, the Municipal Party Department has been asked to send personnel to assist.

Union Asks for Release of Arrested Workers

The strike committee organized by the union found that Gongtai Customs Brokerage was destroying cartage and, during the strike, changed the customs declaration of Tianjin gang goods to Qingdao for transshipment. They sent investigators to persuade them, but it was ineffective. At 12:00 PM yesterday, the Municipal Public Security Bureau sent police to arrest Cheng Pinshun, a worker of the union. It is said that it was to assist the request of the concession police and temporarily detain him in the Public Security Bureau. All the customs brokerage workers were very angry at the Public Security Bureau for arresting workers. The directors and supervisors of the union were deeply afraid of a major disturbance. In addition to advising the workers, they also sent directors to the Social Bureau and the Municipal Party Department to petition for rescue. It is reported that the Municipal Party Department and other departments notified the Public Security Bureau to release the workers because the matter belonged to a labor-management dispute.

Association Reports the Crux of the Dispute

The Transshipment Customs Brokerage Association submitted a document to the Social Bureau for mediation of the dispute, which is recorded as follows: Presentation for reporting matters. The association received a letter from your bureau on the 24th of the previous month, regarding the dispute over cartage for Tianjin gang employees, ordering representatives to come to the bureau for questioning, etc. Following this, on the 25th, we sent representatives Mao Yanling, a committee member, and Wu Yongxia, a public relations officer, to your bureau to await questioning. According to Committee Member Mao and others, they were instructed that the dispute should be mediated by the Association as soon as possible. On the 28th, we first summoned the Tianjin gang to the Association to inquire about the truth of the incident. According to the Tianjin gang associations, including Litaichang, Nangongyi, Yufengsheng, Taichangxiang, and Tongfagong, the cartage fees for customs brokerage employees were initially due to the long distance of shipment and inconvenient transportation. The customers sought quick transportation and had the practice of subsidizing cartage fees. Over time, it became a custom. However, this was obtained by the employees outside, and the customs brokerage never asked about it. In recent years, customers have directly handled goods from foreign firms, and this additional cartage fee is no longer recognized, resulting in threats of strikes by employees once before. As a result, the customers still paid as usual. After the January 28th Incident, Japanese customs brokerages took the opportunity to release the board, waived the cartage fee, and charged customers only 2.84 yuan per piece for shipping. As a result, many customers were greedy for convenience and entrusted the Japanese brokers to handle the shipment. Our association even had no goods to handle and watched the rights and interests flow out. In order to recover, we had to lower the price accordingly. This cartage fee came entirely from the customers, and the customs brokerage could not increase it for the customers, nor could it abolish it for the customers. Taking it would not harm the industry, and abolishing it would not benefit the industry. So why would the industry deprive the employees of their interests and cause meaningless disputes? As for the industry providing employees with monthly salaries and cartage fees for shipments, which are all paid by the industry, the industry has never reduced them because the customers give additional cartage fees. From a rational point of view, the industry has no responsibility for the existence or absence of this unexpected cartage fee. If they use this as a threat, the customers and goods will all fall into the hands of the Japanese, and the result will be the end of the world. Moreover, the current water foot for each piece of foreign cloth, cotton yarn, etc. is only 2.84 yuan collected from the customers. After paying the shipping company 2.52 yuan per piece, the truck fee 0.24 yuan per piece, and the dock workers 0.07 yuan per piece, the industry only has 0.01 yuan left. And the industry's employee salaries and all expenses are still unsettled. The market is so depressed, and the foreign invasion is so great. If our merchants still do not care about the pros and cons and fight each other, driving fish into the deep, it will be painful to say. We will report the whole story to the court. Based on this, Fucha Customs Brokerage and employees, in name, are in the position of capital, but what they rely on for life is all in the customers' goods. As for this additional cartage, according to the association, it comes entirely from the customers. The customs brokerage cannot take it for itself, and the employees do not take it from the customs brokerage. The two parties have no reason to infringe on each other. The reason for the incident is that Japanese customs brokerages release the board and lower prices, and customers flock to them. In order to recover the rights and interests, our customs brokerage has to reduce it accordingly. As a result, the customers also stopped paying the cartage fee, and the employees could not forcefully collect it from the customers. Once they suddenly lost this long-standing benefit, they could not help but vent their anger on the customs brokerage. I think that the most worrying thing at present is not that the dispute is difficult to solve, but that the customers and goods all fall into the hands of Japanese customs brokerages. Even if the industry tries its best to demand the recovery of this cartage fee, who is not greedy for cheap? If the customers and goods are stopped because of this, where can we take it from? The more the labor and management dispute, the more the Japanese industry develops, driving fish into the deep, and the result is the end of the world. This phenomenon should have been seen by your bureau long ago. The Association is in a neutral position and should fulfill its responsibility of mediation. In addition to continuing to summon both labor and management, we will sincerely advise them to eliminate the situation as soon as possible.
