Baoshan County Education Bureau to Hold Exhibition of Self-Made Natural Science Teaching Aids

All Schools Must Prepare Teaching Aids to Send to the Exhibition

The Date of the Exhibition is Determined to be Held During the Summer Vacation

The Baoshan County Education Bureau has initiated the holding of an exhibition of self-made natural science teaching aids, which has been decided to be held during the summer vacation. Everything is currently being prepared, and all schools have been ordered to prepare teaching aids to send to the exhibition. The measures are recorded as follows: (1) The purpose of this exhibition is to exhibit self-made natural science teaching aids from various schools, compare and learn from each other, and increase the interest and teaching efficiency of various schools in making their own natural science teaching aids. (2) All public and private schools in this county must prepare teaching aids to send to the exhibition. (3) All physical objects, specimens, wall charts, models, pictures, charts, instruments, etc. related to natural science are examples collected for exhibition. (4) The exhibition date of this association is set to be during the summer vacation (the exact date will be notified separately). (5) One week before the exhibition period, each school shall send staff to the designated location of the venue to plan and arrange the exhibits. (6) The exhibition location will be notified separately. (7) Each school's products must fill out the following two types of product forms (both issued separately): A. One form per school, filled with the names, numbers, quantities, values, production times, and names of the makers of various self-made teaching aids. B. One sheet per item, filled with the names, numbers, quantities, values, production times, and names of the makers of each school and item. (8) During the exhibition, the bureau will hire judges to evaluate the grades and award prizes separately to encourage. (9) The award methods are divided into two types: A. Cash awards, B. Issuance of certificates of merit. (10) After the opening of the exhibition, the bureau will select the excellent exhibits and send them to the self-made natural science teaching aid exhibition held by the Third District Primary School Education Research Association. The remaining items will be notified to the schools to be collected. (11) All schools may also send teaching aids for other subjects to the exhibition, but a separate venue must be designated.

Shanghai News Agency 1932 Shanghai Education Publishing

Content Encompassing Richness and Half a Million Words

The Shanghai News Agency, renowned in the press for publishing educational news, has recently compiled and printed an educational series to further serve the educational community. It has compiled the events and happenings of the Shanghai educational community in 1933 into a book titled ["Shanghai Education in 1933,"]. This book, one of the series, began compilation by the agency last November. In addition to prefaces written by Minister of Education Wang Shijie and Mayor Wu Tiecheng, over thirty domestic educational figures, including Pan Gongzhan, Zhang Shouyong, Zheng Hongnian, Ye Tianchuo, Chen Heqin, Tao Baichuan, Tao Yuchuan, Yang Weiyu, Zheng Xigu, Shen Siliang, Du Dingyou, Zhou Shang, Chen Bai, Huang Zhaoxiong, Pan Wenan, Jiang Jianbai, Xu Xingchu, Jiang Wenyu, Chen Jicheng, Hu Shuyi, Fu Shishuo, Tong Xingbai, Xu Zexiang, Zhang Zhonghuan, Sun Yuanzeng, Ma Jiazhen, Tang Zeng, Chen Min, Lu Shibai, Zhang Yi, Yu Zhongbiao, and Sun Yusen, Li Bojia, were responsible for the writing. The book also includes inscriptions by Ma Chonggan, Zhu Yixin, and others from various newspapers. Various educational photographs are inserted throughout the text, making it extremely exquisite. The book comprehensively covers the guidelines of Shanghai's educational administration, the state of educational groups, statistics on school education, and special education facilities such as health, hygiene, science, vocational training, children, society, and boy scouts, with meticulous detail. The end of the book includes a record of special events in the education community over the past year, a diary of the education community over the past year, and a directory of large, medium, and small schools in the city. The investigation is detailed, making it particularly valuable. The entire book contains over four hundred pages, encompassing richness and over fifty million words. With its rich content and exquisite printing, it is truly a rare masterpiece in the educational community. All domestic educational organizations, groups, and individuals interested in education should have a copy for reference. The book has already been published and is being sold for two yuan per copy at the agency located at 17 Yingchunfang, Hubei Road. Those who have made advance reservations can bring their reservation vouchers to the agency to collect their copies.

Free Talk

Madwoman

— Lan Ru

It was the second day I went to W City. I found a peculiar woman at the entrance of the hotel. She looked about twenty years old, wearing a purple cotton gown with white floral patterns, her hair was very long and neatly combed, her round face was quite beautiful, but her eyes were a little too sunken, and when she looked at people, she looked as fierce as a tiger about to eat someone; her mouth was always smiling, walking in and out of the hotel entrance, muttering something.

When men passed by, she glared and scolded. When she saw women, she laughed out loud. Immediately, I realized that this was not a character from Simalu, but a mental patient.

During dinner, Mr. Yin told me that the madwoman was the daughter of the hotel manager, a [maiden] who had not yet been betrothed.

After twelve o'clock at night, I suddenly heard the sound of chairs being thrown, doors slamming, followed by shrew-like scolding, the voice fierce and shrill, sometimes almost like a ghost crying. After scolding for a while, she laughed out loud again; before the laughter stopped, she started crying loudly again; after crying, she threw things again, broke glass, opened doors, closed doors, spat in the courtyard: : : It was a complete mess. I wanted to secretly open the door and go out to see what she was doing, but I felt too scared. What if she chased after me? Even if she didn't chase after me, what if she hurt me with something? Wouldn't I be foolishly suffering a loss? There was no way, so I had to grit my teeth and stare at the sky until dawn.

[Were you scared last night?]

Mr. Yin asked me this way when I rinsed my mouth in the courtyard in the morning.

[Amitabha, thank you for telling me, so I was able to get up this morning.]

My words made Te and Lin upstairs laugh out loud.

When we were eating porridge, the madwoman was chewing on a fried dough stick in her mouth. She looked at us and laughed for a while, then scolded for a while. I deliberately clenched my fists and pretended to hit her, but she smiled sweetly at me instead; at this time, we were completely controlled by her and laughed along with her.

It is said that she has been mad for four years. Many people say that this is [Peach Blossom Disease] and that she will only get better after marriage. But heavens, who would dare to marry such a terrifying madwoman as a wife? [Why didn't you marry her off earlier?] I asked them.

[Her father wants to choose a rich man before he will marry her off.] Lin said.

[But rich people want to marry beautiful and flirtatious women, who would want to marry a madwoman?]

[Yes, her father ruined her life!]

The three of them suggested that I say good things to the madwoman's father to get her released. I replied with a smile:

[Whoever is willing to marry her, she will be released.]

There was another burst of laughter.

X X X

The day before yesterday, I received a letter from Mr. Yin, telling me that the crazy girl who had frightened me so much that I couldn't sleep all night had committed suicide! After receiving this news, both Te and I felt sad!

Sailing

— Wen Juan

There is no sun, the northwest wind is blowing coldly, the dark gray sky is putting on an ugly face, and the sea waves are pushing in rows, so our ship starts to shake.

I stood alone on the poop deck looking into the distance, but I saw that the masts were constantly tilting to the left and right, as if they had no stability at all. Whenever a wave hit, a group of passengers would be affected, and the number of people who lost their chopsticks, bowls, and wet bedding gradually increased. They squeezed into the middle, but the middle was not a safe area either. Later, they simply stopped escaping, waiting for the arrival of the waves, and everyone blindly expected the environment to improve itself. But the wind and waves seemed to be joking with these passengers, neither big waves swept them away, nor did it immediately calm down to make them feel at ease. They always teased them like this, with one wave not yet calmed down and another rising again.

In the distance, not even a single sail could be seen on the horizon. Only our lonely boat was struggling to move forward in this desolate sea.

[The symbol of life!] I thought. We take advantage of this lonely boat of life, traveling on this dim sea of life. The fate of the future is unknown, and most of the past is unbearable to recall.

Now, this unfortunate lonely boat is carrying a mission, carrying many lives, to cross the wind and waves and sail to a safe and beautiful place. This work is indeed difficult, but its hull is still strong and its horsepower is sufficient. Even if there are dangerous blows, it cannot be destroyed immediately! Although this journey is indeed a bit too heavy, having a burden can also reduce the emptiness and confusion in its heart. Its only intention now is to break through this gray environment and reach its destination.

Musings

— Xia Chang

(Fifteen)

Yan Shousheng (Pingzi) commented on essays, saying: [These short biographies, short narratives, and short notes are quite pleasing. If they were assigned to write imperial biographies or biographies of famous officials, they would put down their pens. If you talk to them about nature and heaven, they can talk endlessly. If you discuss world affairs with them, they can point out the details and continue endlessly? It's like a small craftsman who builds a small room, a stone bridge, a bamboo path, and arranges it as he pleases. Once entrusted with the Weiyang Palace and the Dew-Collecting Plate, he should stand aside. How different are those frivolous predecessors, who were once powerful, from frogs in a well?] This, of course, represents the views of the orthodox school on essays. It can be said that this view is not based on the quantity of words or the size of the style, but rather on the opposition of the thoughts of the orthodox writers of the Ming Dynasty and the essay writers. In terms of words and styles, there is really no difference.

(Sixteen)

Examining old manuscripts, I found several more short notes, all about life in the rain, which have a similar flavor to the life of the owner of the Bitter Rain Studio today. One is from Mo Tinggan (Qiushui) to Huang Wangzhou, which says: [Embracing depression in the rain, and the noise of human environment, it is extremely difficult for melancholy scholars to express their feelings. When it is slightly sunny, I will go out west and not stop.] The second is from Tinggan to Xu Wenqing: [Although spring rain is beautiful, I regret that it has cut off the communication with my acquaintances. I wonder what you are doing in the studio? If it does not clear up sooner or later, we should meet in person. What books are on the table? I would like to hear about them.] In the latter, the elegant demeanor of a pastoral poet is especially easy to see. However, no one describes life in the rain in more detail than Xu Shipu (Juyuan) to Fan Dashu. It says: [Living in the village and encountering rain, coming and going is cut off from people. Apart from serving food from morning to dusk, even wives and children are rarely seen. Living and planting bamboo, there are occasional bird songs. The low parapet and railing suggest that it is close to the mountains. During the day, I proofread historical books, and at night, I stretch out on a couch. I reject delicacies and stay away from bitter wine. There are no thoughts in my heart, or I may consider the gains and losses of the past and present, and only stamp my foot. After several days like this, the sky will clear up, people will arrive, and I will also go out. It is impossible not to record this. Therefore, I write this by the light of the lamp.] The life of old scholars can be seen from this.

Jilin Folk Song

—

Xi Cun

Riding a donkey,

To my mother's house,

I am not afraid of the long way,

I want to see my parents.

As soon as I enter my mother's house,

There are two people in front and behind,

My brother looks at me,

My sister-in-law twists her body.

[No need to look,

No need to twist,

I won't drink your tea or wine,

I won't eat your rice or meat,

I'll come and go on the same day!]

New Discussion on [Vernacular] [Classical]

— Cao Juren

The discussion on the complexity and simplicity, skill and clumsiness of writing began with the rise of the plain text movement in the Tang and Song dynasties. The "Miscellaneous Notes of the Eight Masters of the Tang and Song Dynasties" records: [When Ouyang Gong was in the Hanlin Academy, he went on a trip with his colleagues. A runaway horse killed a dog on the road. Gong said, "Try to write about this." A colleague said, "A dog was lying in the thoroughfare, and a runaway horse trampled it to death." Gong said, "If you were to write history, ten thousand volumes would not be enough." He said, "What do you think, Intendant?" Gong said, "A runaway horse killed a dog on the road."]

This famous story of the yellow dog and the runaway horse is seen in Shen Kuo's "Dream Pool Essays" and Chen Shan's "New Words While Picking Lice," and the meaning is roughly the same. At that time, the fashion was for scholars to value brevity. The people of the Ming Dynasty advocated restoring the past, and most of them also advocated brevity. It was not until the early Qing Dynasty that scholars began to make ambiguous judgments. Gu Tinglin said: [Words should aim for clarity, regardless of whether they are complex or simple. When the discussion of complexity and simplicity arises, writing dies.] It can be said that it is an extremely insightful view.

Recently, Mr. Lin Yutang advocated the form of recorded sayings, criticizing [modern people writing in vernacular Chinese are just like ancient people writing in parallel prose. They are unwilling to say a truthful word honestly. When they are worried, they say "the trembling of heartstrings," when they are happy, they say "the happiness of happiness," when they are persuaded, they say "accepting opinions," and when they are quick, they say "adding speed." : : : It's just a lot of rambling, and the writing is uneconomical.] (Analects, Issue 26) Rambling is [complex], and economical writing is [simple]. According to Mr. Lin's intention, the shortcoming of vernacular Chinese is complexity, and the strength of the form of recorded sayings is [simplicity]. In this way, we have returned to the old circle of debate over the complexity and simplicity of writing. Around the time of the May Fourth Movement, the promotion of vernacular Chinese generally said that vernacular Chinese was taking spoken language as writing, so that language and writing were close to each other. For more than ten years, the colloquial style has been popular, but the result is not the same. The vernacular Chinese written by women is sometimes hundreds of thousands of miles away from the language of rickshaw pullers and peddlers. For example, the subtitle of [Maternal Light] quoted by Mr. Lin [Her lament, her tears of blood, the audience's sympathy and sorrow, the tension of heartstrings - just at this time of lament, tears of blood, the audience's sympathy and sorrow, the tension of heartstrings, the embroidered curtain slowly fell] - to rickshaw pullers and peddlers, it is no easier than [Zixu Rhapsody and Shanglin Rhapsody]. Another example is a famous line from a certain poet [Ode to Pomegranate Flowers]: [The more the pomegranate flowers bloom, the redder they are, the redder they cannot be.] And the [Chinese Christians in Gulangyu, Xiamen bow three times to the portrait of Sun Yat-sen, considering it inconsistent with the Tongmenghui], all make people feel that the vernacular is too rambling. Why is vernacular Chinese often so rambling? Where is the difference between vernacular and classical Chinese? Is there a need to advocate the form of recorded sayings? We should re-examine these questions. (To be continued)

Spring on the Lake

— Hei Ying

The train arrived in Hangzhou.

My heart was tightly entangled in a beautiful dream: Where is West Lake? I was so eager to see this scenic spot in Jiangnan!

I got on a rickshaw and went to the lakeside. - A line of seventeen people, seventeen rickshaws connected and ran through the streets of Hangzhou. I thought: The spring in Hangzhou is sunny, the wind is gentle: my nineteen-year-old heart should be happy here too, right?

Happy spring!

I couldn't help but shout when I saw West Lake for the first time.

- Don't you want to eat?

- Let's go boating on the lake! Let's go boating on the lake!

Overcoming hunger, five of us walked together to the lake. - The lake surface was still, and slight ripples tightly trailed behind the painted boats; the willows on the embankment swayed in the wind, and a gust of floral fragrance from I don't know where made me a little drunk standing on the lakeside.

We called a boat and all five of us got on. The warm sun shone on our heads, the leisurely lake water rippled under our feet, and there were the green hills on the opposite side, and the tower on the mountain stood there smiling like a giant. The boat left the shore and rowed towards the center of the lake, lightly and driftingly, and we were all silent for a while.

We rowed to Huxin Pavilion, and then to Three Pools Mirroring the Moon.

- Let's go up and take a look!

We all followed Miss X's advice and jumped ashore together. Surrounded on all sides by lake water: many birds were chirping on the branches. There were many words and paintings there, and Hangzhou's special products of lotus root flour and lotus root starch were sold. Miss X bought some and hung them on her hands, then returned to the boat.

We were all laughing on the lake: our hearts were happy and relaxed: : :

But, I don't know when, the dark clouds in the sky gradually thickened, and the sunlight had disappeared. When the boat rowed to Autumn Moon over the Calm Lake, thin lines of rain began to fall on our bodies.

- It's raining! What to do?

- Let's hide for a while, go up there: : :

- Let's row! Let everyone get wet!

Yes, the rain couldn't stop our interest in the lake, and the boatman had no choice but to continue rowing towards the lake.

The rainy West Lake has a different flavor! Misty, covered with a layer of fog, Three Pools Mirroring the Moon and Huxin Pavilion half-hid their faces. After a while, the rain still hadn't stopped, and the calligraphy and paintings in Miss X's hand were all wet!

- Are you cold?

She asked me.

- A little: : :

Until dusk, the five of us returned to the hostel with wet and tired bodies. Looking at each other, we couldn't help but laugh.

Tentative Translation of the Book of Songs

— Yu Shi Xia

Going out of the East Gate

One

Going out of this east gate for a stroll,

There are as many girls as clouds.

Although there are as many as clouds,

They are not in my heart.

Still the white clothes and blue turban,

She makes me feel happy.

Two

Going out of this east gate, I want it,

The girls are as beautiful as camellias.

Although they are as beautiful as camellias,

I never thought about her.

Still the white clothes and crimson dress,

I can have a pleasant chat with her.

Half a Day's Lessons (4)

— Li Huiying

Hearing her words, I thought of Mr. Zhang, who was taken away by Japanese soldiers during the incident. It has been two years since we parted with Mr. Zhang. I don't know where she went. Such a good teacher who taught us cannot be found now. Comparing what she said before with the principal's words, there is a world of difference. What is called [new education]? Is it calling the Japanese "grandpa"? Is it honestly preparing to be a subjugated slave? This evil wild chicken, she is really a complete Japanese lackey! In a few years, it is said that a large number of submissive people will be created in the same school. At that time, the students will definitely forget that they were originally a part of the oppressed Chinese nation.

After that, I didn't hear anything she said, but I guessed from her first paragraph of training that the script must have been written for her by someone else. Otherwise, even two sentences, she wouldn't be able to say them so logically and use the words so appropriately.

After a while, she finished speaking, and the schoolboy brought several bundles of small paper national flags. The small flagpoles were only a little over a foot long, and the flag paper rustled in the wind. Each student was given a flag. The director of discipline came to speak again. After he finished speaking, we were led by him and set off in formation.

However, I remembered that interesting sentence of his and thought about it while walking. He said to the students like that:

[Don't think that going to the meeting is for fun. Actually, it's just like going to class!]

That's right, I can't remember how many times I've taken such lessons in the past two years. Often, when a Japanese official comes, we students will be ordered to go to the station to welcome him. This is a new lesson in the new education.

Following the Mongolian Banner Hutong, our team walked towards Weixin Street. The small flags in everyone's hands were all fluttering in the wind. On the contrary, everyone's psychology was lifeless. Therefore, the director of discipline shouted loudly:

[Why are you all so dejected? What are you thinking?]

When the team reached Xinkaimen Street, a team of students blocked the way. These were students from the Women's Normal School. Like us, they all had a small national flag in their hands. The people watching the excitement on the side of the street stood like two walls. At this time, I felt a little hot, unlike the weather on the car, which was still a bit cold.

The sky was humming, and three Japanese planes were flying from north to south. Afterwards, things fell from the sky like snow, flipping and flying, and it took a long time to fall to the ground. These were leaflets, both in Chinese and Japanese. Some children squeezed and snatched in the crowd, as if they had found some treasure.

The poor children only knew how to grab the leaflets, but they didn't know what was printed on them. They didn't even know that they were slaves of a fallen country. Naturally, they didn't have to worry about these things. Their parents were all coolies, who only knew how to run around for a living every day, only knew how to fill their stomachs, and had no time to think about the survival of the country! They didn't care about these things. Whether there was a country or not, they still lived a life of poverty. Their children, of course, also didn't pay attention to the rise and fall of the country.

US Tacit Approval of Silver Bill May Make It Difficult for the Gold Market to Sustain

Despite Central Bank Buying Over a Thousand Bullion Bars

Frequent Selling by Major Players Leads to a Fall of Three Yuan

Yesterday, the gold market ultimately struggled to sustain itself due to frequent reports of adverse news from overseas. The afternoon market was relatively calm. Initially, the overseas silver market saw a united pullback in both British and American markets. The five metals exchange saw forward silver prices rise by nearly four hao to one li three, and fall by as much as one li one. Exchange rates have already shown a pullback. London spot gold fell eleven pence, US cotton rose six points, and US wheat rose one point. Wool futures opened and immediately rose to 57 yuan. Subsequently, due to Associated Press reports mentioning the proposal to raise silver prices, gains were limited. After opening, the HSBC exchange rate suddenly contracted, leading to a period of strength. Although the Central Bank then vigorously entered the market with over a thousand bullion bars, an Associated Press report stated that the US government, in light of congressional opposition to the Canadian hydroelectric power project, might use the silver bill as a bargaining chip. If the bill were to pass, the government would likely take action to raise silver prices. Major players such as Cheng Feng Yong continuously sold off their holdings, causing gold prices to decline repeatedly. Later in the day, the market stabilized as banks showed a strong appetite for purchases. However, market conditions were generally mediocre, with the price of pure gold quoted at 971 yuan. Native Bank Business Declines

Both Collection and Settlement Transactions are Stagnant

In recent days, following the foreign banks' closure, business was only slightly busier on the reopening day. Subsequently, due to weak market sentiment and a lack of substantial prosperity, lending became difficult, and funds were not easily deployed. Ultimately, the market became sparsely populated, and morale waned. Foreign interbank lending rates remained unchanged, at five percent for both the morning and afternoon markets. Overdraft facilities also remained unavailable, with all transactions settled in cash. Transactions involving interbank lending bills amounted to 4.2 to 4.3 million yuan for transfers in the morning market and 700,000 to 800,000 yuan for new transactions. Afternoon transactions totaled just over 300,000 yuan, and transactions in the small general association were only slightly over 400,000 yuan. Transactions involving foreign collateral loans saw limited activity in real estate, with only goods and securities being used as collateral. As a result, the amount was not significant, with redemptions and new loans totaling just over 1.3 to 1.4 million yuan. Transactions involving banknotes totaled just over 1.5 million yuan. In terms of bank collections and settlements, foreign banks collected and settled bill payments totaling 1.4 to 1.5 million yuan, and various goods, exchange, collateral, and miscellaneous payments totaling 3.0 million yuan. Direct offsets for warehouse receipts and releases totaled 600,000 yuan. Chinese banks collected and settled bill payments totaling 1.9 million yuan, and various goods, exchange, tax, collateral, and miscellaneous payments totaling 4.2 million yuan, with warehouse releases of 600,000 yuan. Japanese banks collected and settled bill payments totaling 1.7 to 1.8 million yuan, and various goods, exchange, and miscellaneous payments totaling 2.8 million yuan, with warehouse releases of 400,000 yuan. Native banks collected and settled foreign public orders totaling over 38 million yuan, foreign overdraft payments totaling over 6.3 million yuan, various remittance payments totaling over 300,000 yuan, cash collections of 800,000 to 900,000 yuan, and incoming customer funds of 200,000 yuan. Outgoing funds were limited, with only 150,000 yuan going to the Yangtze River region. Furthermore, the total number of exchanges at the local clearinghouse on the 5th was 8,265,352.33 yuan, including 4,900,969.77 yuan in silver dollars and 3,356,182.56 yuan in interbank transfers.

Guangdong Coins Fall and Copper Coins Contract Again

Yesterday, Jiangnan small silver coins remained unchanged in both the morning and afternoon markets, maintaining the previous day's price of 833 yuan. Transactions were limited, with only 5,000 jiao in the morning market and a standstill in the afternoon market. Guangdong small silver coins appeared to have fallen slightly, by 1.1 yuan, compared to the previous day, with the price quoted at 755.7 yuan in both the morning and afternoon markets. Transactions totaled 45,000 jiao in the morning market and 20,000 jiao in the afternoon market. Copper coins contracted by 2,000 wen, to 320,500 wen, with 32,050 strings transacted, representing a value of 10,000 yuan.

Securities US Bonds Rise Sharply

Xin Feng Foreign Company reported yesterday on the New York stock market, stating that fluctuations were slight and somewhat uneven. The Treasury Department's fourth free public debt exchange plan was proceeding along the proper channels, strengthening the US dollar. However, several stocks broke records due to special circumstances, and low-priced stocks were particularly active. Market conditions on the small exchange were firm and bullish, with the largest gains reaching around 5 yuan. Bonds rose sharply due to the Treasury Department's announcement, with US bonds up half a yuan and railroad bonds rising several jiao to 3 yuan. The company's New York agent also reported that (securities) were sluggish but uneven, with slight gains. (Wheat) Rumors of silver inflation were rampant, causing short sellers to cover their positions, and market conditions appeared to be trending higher. (Cotton) Buyers' confidence was gradually increasing. The Punkhae case was currently facing opposition, but supporters of the case predicted that it would have a successful outcome. Inflationists in Congress continued their activities. The exchange case was facing strong opposition and would likely be amended again. Russian demand remained a significant potential force. Spot prices were quiet, and trading was stable, with purchases advisable during periods of weakness. The total volume traded for the day was 1.56 million shares. The Dow Jones Index is listed below:

Yarn and Cloth The Current Yarn and Cloth Market is Incredibly Dull

The yarn market remains lackluster and uninspired, lacking any excitement. There is no trading in yarn futures due to the market closure. The number of people gathering in the market is as scarce as the morning stars. Although foreign cotton has seen a slight increase, it has had no impact, primarily due to the poor environment and sluggish actual sales. Furthermore, foreign merchants are dumping their goods everywhere, making it even more difficult for Chinese yarn to gain a foothold. According to statistics, all gangs bought a total of 194 bales for the day. There was no change in market conditions. The purchase amounts for each gang are as follows:

US Cotton Rises Slightly Due to Short Covering

Yesterday, US cotton initially weakened due to selling by foreign merchants, but then strengthened due to favorable conditions in the cloth market and short covering. As a result, spot prices rose by five points, and futures prices rose by five to seven points. British cotton spot prices fell by five points, and futures prices rose by one point. Egyptian cotton spot prices fell by seven points. Indian cotton was stagnant and unremarkable, with Pingguor falling by one and a half rupees, Omla falling by one rupee and seven and a half jiao, and Bairoxi falling by half a rupee. Although the 包胃 of 青角松泗西练 and other late rice varieties continued to move, as the 北洋帮 did not show a weakening interest, only purchasing 1,400 to 1,500包, it was still difficult for market conditions to improve, so prices remained stable. The 去路 of 杜羊尖 turned dull, showing slight softness, but prices still showed no ups or downs. Both 阴变元供求 were rare, and prices were still balanced.

Soybeans Sluggish Sales Continue to Fall

Raw Peanuts Opened with 2,000 Bags

Yesterday, the soybean market continued to decline. The source of goods was continuous but not surging, and the demand from factories was also weak. Market sentiment was fluctuating, and prices continued to fall by two to three points. The future prospects are feared to be more declines than gains. Yesterday, a total of 200 bags of 正阳关 beans were traded, purchased by exporters in this street. Two cars of 归德 beans were opened, and distributed by domestic merchants in this street. 350 bags of 颖州 beans and 400 bags of 肥河 beans were opened, all processed by merchants in this street. There were also 100 bags of Dalian Sipingjie beans, which were reportedly taken by domestic merchants. The raw peanut market, after a temporary increase due to reports of rising产地 prices, has returned to sluggishness as Cantonese merchants only buy at low prices. Reportedly, two batches were opened the night before, including more than 1,000 bags of 州山货 at a price of 3.55 yuan, and over 900 bags of 州货 at a price of 3.45 yuan.

High Quality Late Rice Already Opened at 8.1 Yuan

Small Amount of Hunan Rice Has Recently Arrived in Shanghai

Yesterday, the arrival and inventory of 客秈 were both low, and all transactions were active, with prices continuing to rise. High-quality 江西機晚 rice reached 8.1 yuan yesterday. The owners of Hunan and other high-quality goods have set price limits at the产地 and did not allow for cheap sales. However, a small amount of 中关湘米 has recently been装到, and the quantity is not large. Furthermore, a portion of it is also sold with price limits, so transactions have not been robust. All day, 福州 purchased 350 bags of 機晚, 394 bags of 機靖米, 215 bags of 沙市糙米, and 380 bags of 芜湖機秈. High-quality goods, such as 機晚米, rose by nearly a 角, and all other 中次 grades continued to rise by five to seven or eight points. This street has not inquired about 客秈 due to its high price and has only purchased a small amount of 绞 at a price of 8.75 yuan.

Sugar Market Taikoo Sugar Prices Are Gradually Tightening

Yesterday, the trend in the sugar market was relatively stable, with the volume of trade remaining unexceptional. The公会划盘 prices for 24th grade coarse granulated white sugar were 19.85 yuan for ordinary 本栈货 and 19.9 yuan for 转口货, with little change. There was also a lack of movement for 8th and 9th grade 荷赤. The prices for Taikoo Sugar B rose by five points to 20.3 yuan. The prices for other grades such as CW were 19.95 yuan, DY 19.7 yuan, and HX 19.45 yuan, all of which saw some trading. The prices for the 本厂绵白振记 1st grade were 18.4 yuan, the same price as 金心 1st grade. The prices for the remaining 2nd, 3rd, and 4th grades were discounted. There was little opening for the 号盘, with 枝洋 priced at 14.75 yuan, without much upward momentum. Hainan赤 sales showed activity, and the situation for the 号盘 was not loose.

North-South Goods Longkou Vermicelli New Goods Will Arrive Soon

Market Prices Are Gradually Loosening

Longkou vermicelli sales have been sluggish recently. In addition, new goods will arrive soon, so the market trend is gradually declining. The opening prices for 客货 have also loosened, decreasing by approximately one yuan compared to before, but the 走场 is still not smooth. Oil Market White Tung Oil Hankou Prices Rise Again

In Hankou, the 洋庄 trading of white tung oil has been continuous for days, while the supply remains scarce, resulting in an increasingly tight market. After the 洋行箱 entered the market at 25 yuan, telegraphs yesterday reported that it had been sold at 25.7 yuan, and the situation remained tight, with the possibility of further increases. The recent免起鹘落 in Hankou 洋庄 tung oil is not uncommon. However, the price rises quickly and the price falls easily. The current situation is slightly different from the past because the price increase is not drastic, rising gradually, and therefore seems more stable than rapid increases. It is not as easy to compare with rapid rises and falls. However, now that the market has risen to this point, it seems unlikely that it will rise further, but a small increase is still possible. The root is stable, and it would not be easy for the prices to fall, as the basics are solid and it would be very difficult to turn the market down. It is reported that Hankou 行 opened and purchased 客货, with 襄桐 priced around 21 yuan, and 南支 at 20.78 yuan. The quantity coming is not large and there are no large volume purchases. Zhejiang tung followed Hankou tung and gradually increased. According to yesterday's news, 杭行 sold and delivered at 21.4 yuan per stone, and 金兰 various產地 have also seen increases, so its rising wind is still flourishing. There have been a few 洋庄 transactions in the local area recently, done by a certain soybean and rice merchant, with a transaction volume of about dozens of tons. In terms of inbound cargo, this can be said generally true, with a few 桐油号家 trading in 洋庄货. Sales have been slight recently, but in even smaller amounts. Domestic sales remain scattered, so despite the rise in Hankou, they are still unable to be more active in inbound cargo.

Silk and Tea Foreign Sales of Chinese Silk are Stagnant

New York Raw Silk Sales Decrease Sharply New York silk weaving factories, due to the global economic panic, have seen sluggish sales of silk fabrics, with full silk fabric inventories, so they are 工停机. Raw silk sales have decreased sharply. Yesterday, 美丝 received a telegraph from the New York silk market stating that in the past month (i.e., March), silk weaving factories in New York City only consumed a total of 28,394 packages of raw silk, only about 5/10 of that of months in previous years.

Ji Li Dried Silk Sales to the US are Terminated The superior Ji Li Dried Silk produced in Zhejiang and Hubei enjoyed strong sales in the US. In recent years, due to poor manufacturing, it has been almost entirely infringed upon by Japanese silk sales. Ji Li Dried Silk has become extinct in the New York market. This year, no Dried Silk was shipped to the US in the first three months. Recently, there were only three packages of Huzhou Baitusi shipped to Seattle, reportedly new silk samples.

Yangzhuang Silk Market is Lifeless The overseas raw silk market has a large raw silk inventory, and consumption is decreasing daily. The actual sales in Lyon and other places are stagnant, and New York silk prices will be difficult to sustain. The import merchants are eager to sell their raw silk inventory, but the Shanghai factory has not responded to the telegraph. The Yangzhuang silk market is still lifeless. Yesterday, only Dachang and others purchased ten packages of 黄厂经 and five packages of 灰经, but prices remained depressed.

Shanghai News Additional Supplement

Casual Remarks

On the Issue of Prisoners' Sexual Desires

— Yafei

The day before yesterday, all the newspapers competed to publish a fresh piece of news: [A Reuters dispatch from Guangzhou Nanhiong authorities recently received a petition from prisoners sentenced to long-term imprisonment, requesting that the authorities allow the prisoners' families to enter the prison on time to cohabitate, so as to pass on descendants. The petition also cited Confucius' saying, "There are three unfilial acts, and having no descendants is the greatest." It is heard that the authorities intend to reject this request, believing that Chinese judicial system does not have a provision that a prisoner's wife can enter the prison to cohabitate with her husband:]: etc.

This piece of news is truly extremely novel and strange. I do not know whether the various civilized countries already have explicit regulations that a prisoner's wife can enter the prison on a regular basis to cohabitate with her husband? If there is such a fact, then, I think the judicial authorities, in addition to building prisons, should also build a number of secret rooms, so that those prisoners' wives can enter the prison on a regular basis to cohabitate with their husbands, so that they can pass on the family line. This would be immeasurable merit and a virtue of cherishing life.

The use of Confucius' saying, "There are three unfilial acts, and having no descendants is the greatest," as a banner in the petition, I think they are worthy of having [read Confucius' books] and [reached the rites of the Duke of Zhou]. Indeed, even though they are in prison, they still diligently remember to pass on the family line. It can be seen that they are indeed great filial sons (?): admirable, admirable! However, did Confucius consider this for prisoners when he said this? If not, then I cannot help but speak up for the injustice he suffered. However, I also thought of those prisoners who are not married, what methods should they use to pass on the family line? This is a major issue.

A long time ago! I remember that Luo Wengan once published an opinion on the issue of liberating prisoners' sexual desires. At that time, it also caused the newspapers to publish it. He had already submitted the main idea and motive of this issue to the Executive Yuan for approval, and planned to first implement it on a trial basis in inland prisons, and then promote it nationwide after it was confirmed that no malpractices occurred. [For prisoners sentenced to long-term imprisonment, if it is determined that they have a marital relationship, they may cohabitate in prison within a specified period.] After this news came out, there were criticisms from the general public. The reason is that prisoners' behavior is bad, and the transmission of their bad heredity, even if conception occurs, will not produce a good race. Moreover, at that time, both parties were in a depressed and sad environment, and their thoughts may not have been happy. In the future, the impact on the future of the race is not small. Whether their families are willing to enter the prison and cohabitate with them is another question, but the limitations of time are also an unavoidable fact.

Later, Luo's proposal was not approved by the Executive Yuan, so it dissipated into smoke and became a bubble. Over time, everyone gradually forgot about this matter. Now, the prisoners in Guangzhou have unexpectedly submitted such a petition, which can be said to be in response to Luo's proposal. Unfortunately, however, it was strongly rejected by the Guangzhou authorities; this is like a bucket of cold water pouring down from the top of their heads, chilling all their hopes.

However, I also heard that in the Japanese legal system, there is indeed such a fact. If a prisoner is sentenced to imprisonment for more than one year, his family members can go to a designated secret room every week to have a rendezvous with her husband. But, I don't know if it is a fact?

My Hometown

— Naishuo

My hometown is not Xiangxiang, but the small Yongfeng.

In Xiangxiang County, under the fame of Zeng Xiangxiang, the county town is so desolate and deserted. The rows of shops are only the residences of merchants, and they cannot create the outline of a commercial city. Yongfeng, although it is such a small town, has a strong commercial force. It has the convenience of boats and ships on the water, and cars speeding on land, and it also controls a military stronghold. Although there are not many shops || equivalent to Jiangwan Town, its substance is more than ten times better.

It was exactly ten years ago, in the early autumn, that I went to Yongfeng to study at a high school thirty miles away from the neighboring town. Speaking of this high school, it is not like the small elementary schools in Shanghai with one or two floors or even only a pavilion room. It is simply better than the general middle schools in Shanghai. It has spacious school buildings and hundreds of acres of foundation. The Girls' Vocational School facing the river is so mysterious! Their power is truly boundless. I remember that in our boys' school in those years, there was such a prohibition: [In the evening, students are not allowed to linger on the opposite bank of the girls' school when they go out for a walk.] Speaking of our high school, it has educated many people.

Many revolutionary generals of the contemporary era have visited and stayed in our Yongfeng, and sown countless revolutionary seeds. We even personally welcomed the troops and provided food and drink. We climbed on the generals' carriages and received their kind nods and smiles. We even went crazy and propagated all over the streets. I remember in those years, our pure hearts only had the illusion of hoping for the success of the revolution!

The commerce there is surprisingly prosperous, with southern goods piled up like mountains, Jiangxi's large pharmacies, and transfer companies. It is the central point for local products from all over, and also the distribution point for foreign goods. When it dawns, the citizens crowd the streets like a swarm of bees. Late at night, in addition to the sound of the watchman's clapper, you can also subtly appreciate the night pilgrimage of the local opera troupe. There has never been a famine, so I don't know what it means to be in a recession.

Comparatively speaking, it seems like a pure country girl with a sacred heart, only seeing the exuberant joy of life, and no deep atmosphere of dusk.

This is the scene from ten years ago.

It has also become the scene from ten years ago, it's the past!

And now, it is truly [unbearable to look back on those years]! Last year, I went back, and I only had an excited mood along the way. Who knew that after meeting, it was so surprising!

A lively and bustling city has turned into a desolate and deserted market, and the original shops, although they are still struggling to maintain themselves, everyone has reached the tip of decline.

On the street, you can only see dogs fighting, and the roofs are where crows and magpies crow. The prosperity of ten years ago has disappeared to who knows where.

What is new is that whenever a car drives into the station, there are more groups of vendors shouting, more semi-Westernized hotels and warehouses, and a group of Western-suited teenagers strolling on the street.

Recently, I have received several pieces of news from my hometown, all saying that it has become like an old woman who is about to die.

Recently, I have also met several fellow villagers who have just fled from their hometown. As soon as we meet and talk about Yongfeng, everyone can only shake their heads. They don't talk about the decline of the countryside or the recession of the market, but only say in unison:

[One round of war and one round of disaster, my hometown is unbearable to inquire about!]

Returning Late from Bai Causeway

— Qingmu

A round of maiden-like delicate sun has shyly hidden behind the peak over there. Slices of colorful clouds, rich in curves, also seem to be eagerly seeking a partner to find their home. At that time, Bai Causeway was covered with fragrant and beautiful footprints, and pairs of young men and women, talented scholars and beautiful women, were holding hands and talking sweetly under the shade of the willow trees by the causeway. The cunning fish in the lake also learned from them, whispering to each other, lingering and reluctant to leave, truly envying us single men.

Generally, old ladies and pilgrims, hanging yellow sachets, returned from Lingyin and Tianzhu temples after offering incense, praying for more fortune and longevity, and for offspring to be successful. I lonely tour this scenic spot on the causeway, Fanghe Pavilion, Autumn Moon over the Calm Lake, Xiling Seal Engravers' Society, which only added to my sorrow. This was originally a place for poets and hermits to taste tea and write poetry, but now, it is crowded with people and full of vulgarity, like a teahouse on the sea! They were originally enough to add color to the lake and mountains, but now they have become superfluous.

The moon is gradually rising, which is a sign that prompts me to return. I haven't walked so much today, but at this time I already feel tired and exhausted, how useless. Tomorrow I must get up early to look at the beautiful scenery of the Qiantang River sunrise from the Wangyang Terrace. Although there will be another opportunity tomorrow, but where in our life is there any hope for the future, except for what has already arrived before our eyes.

In an unguarded moment, suddenly the lingering sounds from the guesthouse opposite our room that had been tightly closed yesterday promoted my eardrums. I don't know what kind of magic power it seemed to attract my attention. I looked down from the gap in the window, but only a very blurry phantom-like phenomenon was printed into my eyes, like a pair of angel-like lovers, embracing and kissing tightly. From the movements on their appearance, I am afraid that they are not a formal pair of mandarin ducks? Such enthusiasm, I am afraid, will also envy the Bodhisattva in the Buddha Hall over there, let alone us single men: but I already know love, love that can now be bought with gold!

Ah, love, I advise you to stop talking about love!

Do you have plenty of gold in your pocket?

If you are still a poor scholar,

I advise you not to tease the flirtatious!

Reading Notes from the Shen Bao Circulating Library

— Guanghan

The Shen Bao Circulating Library was established on the third floor of the Continental Emporium on Nanjing Road. Although it has only been open for more than a year, the results have been quite impressive. Because the location is suitable and the transportation is convenient, it is extremely crowded every day with people who come to the library to borrow books or read magazines and newspapers. Although my residence is far from this place, I am always in the habit of running to the library whenever I go out for something or when I am bored, and casually flipping through a few pages of magazines or newspapers. Last Wednesday afternoon, I made a special [visit] to spend most of the day.

After receiving a copper tag from the entrance, I selected an issue of the "Eastern Miscellany" from the bookshelf and settled down in an empty seat in the reading room. Before I opened the book to read, I raised my head and looked around. Today, there are probably more than twenty readers. There are those who look like students, those who are in the professional world, and those who are dressed like workers. [A touch of red amidst the green], coincidentally, among many men, there is a lady mixed in. They are either sitting or standing, reading magazines or newspapers, and pairs of eyes are all focused on the books and volumes arranged on the table or held in their hands, as if they are looking for some secret.

After I finished reading the two articles I wanted to read, I wanted to find another piece of literature that I wanted to read, but it was gone, it had already been taken by someone who was faster. So I went to the borrowing desk to fill out a borrowing slip, hoping to borrow one or two volumes of social sciences to read, but unexpectedly, I wrote four book titles in a row, but none of them were borrowed. Helpless, I had to flip through the daily newspapers. After a while, I borrowed a copy of "China's Grand View" to read. People left and came to the reading room for a while, and more people came than left.

The time was already 5:25, and I felt mentally exhausted, so I returned the copper tag and stepped out of the reading room. At this moment, there were still many people standing outside the window waiting to borrow books, and the clerks in the library looked very busy.

In the elevator, a question suddenly popped into my mind: Why don't these people go to the amusement park to have fun when they are free, but instead come here to sit and ponder, and stare at the books in a daze? Oh! I understand, it turns out that human life, in addition to material sustenance, also needs spiritual food. Spiritual hunger is as uncomfortable as emptiness in the stomach. And the library is a place to provide [spiritual food], no wonder countless people with a desire for knowledge like to run here, hoping to get some spiritual satisfaction from here.

The Shen Bao Circulating Library, this [public spiritual canteen], is a social enterprise held by Shen Bao on the occasion of its 60th anniversary. This [canteen] is providing nutrients to a group of people with spiritual famine, which is very beneficial to the public. We hope that it can expand and develop day by day, and prepare a variety of [rare delicacies and fine wines] in abundance, so as to feast the general [hungry and thirsty], so that people in society will not feel the risk of spiritual cold and hunger, then the contribution to culture will not be small!

On Women's Sports

— Ms. Jiong

For thousands of years, women have been confined by stale and antiquated traditions. Apart from being deeply imprisoned in the family, serving as slaves and beasts of burden, they had no way to create and develop their own urgent undertakings. Where would they have the leisure to discuss sports, which they considered an extra issue, and to actually practice it? Because at that time, strict feudal ideas bound their minds. Except for a small number of women, most simply did not know this term existed. Some even thought that it was not something women could enjoy. It seemed that the social system at that time had already predetermined women's fate. It was not considered unfortunate for them to be deprived of this right, and it was even considered a matter of course. Women could only stay in the depths of their boudoirs, serving as beasts of burden and slaves to men!

With the eastward spread of European customs and after several waves of women's movements, the old system gradually collapsed along with this turbulent current. All kinds of new phenomena rose up. The call for women's sports and the advocacy of women's sports became increasingly responsive. The derogatory terms previously used such as "sick women of the East" and "sickly beauties" were replaced with a new requirement for healthy beauty. Objectively, we certainly cannot deny the astonishing progress of women's sports in recent years! Women's sports competitions have been successively launched in various provinces and counties, and women compatriots who have been imprisoned in dark hells for thousands of years have been promoted to the battlefield one after another, demonstrating their respective skills. In particular, last year's grand and magnificent National Games, which cost tens of thousands of capital, built a solemn and majestic sports field in Nanjing. Each province selected so many amazing female heroes to perform on the field. We cannot deny the general factual proof of the progress of women's sports. This time, the international women's basketball team, with their intelligence and courage, and with their hearts and minds exhausted, defeated Britain by a score of thirty-four to twenty-seven, and regained the international women's championship in this city, not falling into the hands of blue-eyed people, which is really gratifying. Such earth-shattering progress, in the current state of extreme decline of national spirit, cannot but be said to be a new phenomenon. Especially for the just budding future of women's sports, what a fortunate thing is it?

As a result of the poor social organization, all phenomena are deformed and morbid. Although the above mentioned some facts about the development and progress of women's sports, how many places and schools are still waiting for this kind of facility! Therefore, although women's sports have some achievements, they have not progressed to all places and spread to the generally oppressed women:

Art is a beautiful phenomenon that restores people's fatigue; similarly, sports are also aimed at strengthening the body. At present, because of the unsound general system and organization, sports have not been soundly implemented in every individual, but are deformed and partial. In particular, women's sports are a very obvious fact.

In many villages not far from the cities, can we not often see women who have lost their natural feet, passed down from thousands of years of tradition, still suffering there, suffering from this genetic disease? Therefore, we know that the so-called development of women's sports is just a modern slogan and decoration for a part of the people in the city.

We should absolutely advocate sports, especially women's sports, which is a matter of urgency and needs to be revitalized! In the future, how should we popularize women's sports so that women who have been oppressed and imprisoned in jail-like conditions for thousands of years can enjoy this right and embark on the road to health!

On Women

— Qing

Women are naturally born for men, and men can never do without women. The relationship between the two is understood even by children, so there is no need to say more. The existence of women is like a shadow following the body, and they cannot be separated in any way. If there were no women to embellish the world, it would become a desolate desert. Not only would men not be able to survive, but humanity would have ended long ago. So when you talk about women, when you see women, you always can't help but smile and become excited for no reason, unless you are a piece of insensitive wood. Indeed, women are the source of life, more important than firewood and rice, the world would not be the world without them, the magic of women is incredible. Every frown and smile of a woman is worth a thousand gold pieces, but its harm often arises from this, the so-called benefit must have its drawbacks. Often for that light frown and smile, you are so mesmerized that you throw all the big things to the back of your mind, even if you die or your family is ruined, you don't care. There is even the saying that "one glance can overthrow a city, and another glance can overthrow a country." In history, many昏庸昏庸kings have lost their country and extinct their race because of a mere woman's body. Some people often only think that "beautiful colors are important in the world," and raise women up to the clouds, willing to be cattle and horses under pomegranate skirts, wholeheartedly indulging in the beauty's den. And they have never thought about the terrible harm that women can cause. Knowing that it is drinking poison to quench thirst, they still drink it indifferently, and die without realizing it. Even if they are harmed by women and become fragmented, desolate and miserable, they still do not regret it, but still worship them, chase them, and enshrine them as sacred and dignified objects. This is truly worthy of tears.

Women are certainly very necessary, but it is necessary to add considerable contempt to them, and not to regard them as so mysterious and so noble, so that they can reflect more and dare not forget to be proud and reserved, and regard themselves as great figures. Because if you value them too much, they will look down on everything and ride you as a beast of burden. Moreover, you are a human being, are you willing to use your majestic seven-foot body as a beast of burden, and not feel ashamed?

Women are indeed naturally beautiful things, more harmful than beneficial. Since they cannot be dispensed with, and cannot be too much, it is really a bit like chicken ribs, tasteless to eat, but a pity to throw away. They are very good at being妖妖冶冶. If you are too considerate and polite, she will actually climb on your head and defecate. Of course, I do not absolutely slander women. I have always kept myself pure, and do not learn from the mad bees and wandering butterflies. Therefore, I have never been fooled by women, and I am not qualified to talk about unrequited love. So my relationship with women can be said to be without hatred or resentment, without hatred or love. However, I often see a group of people serving women almost as if they were serving their ancestors and parents, with the feeling that "everything else is inferior, only women are good," doing their best to endure humiliation. What I have heard and witnessed makes me feel infinitely感嘆. People's hearts are not ancient, and rivers are declining day by day. I am really disgusted, so I will do some counter-articles, so that "those who only know that there are women and do not know that there are other things, the only-womenists, do not live such a confused life,糊裏糊塗 making women's sacrifices, leaving a bad name for ten thousand years. Women are certainly important, but also remember that women can call people to ruin their reputation and die without a burial place. For this, if you can taste it carefully, there is a great truth in it, and you can gain endless benefits, and make you change your improper respect for women."

Amateur Mailbox

From Venereal Diseases to Youthful Sexual Frustration

｜Editor's Note｜

Three letters discussing this issue have already been published, and the remaining letters will not be published because their meanings are similar. Moreover, this discussion has been going on for more than a week. Even if the readers are not tired of it, they are probably eagerly awaiting the editor to draw a conclusion with an "old face"! It is also very ashamed to say that I dare not say what I wanted to say with an old face now, I am a little shy, because if everyone does not feel depressed about this issue, the world and the sexual depression, that is, the depression is not to seek catharsis from indulgence, the solution is very easy, but if the depression is inevitable, the sexual desire has no reasonable solution, then it is difficult. Therefore, although the editor's previous views on this issue are still not considered wrong by himself, he is still a little unsure whether it can prevent young people from taking this risk again. Why? Because this issue is not an independent issue, but is caused by the current social chaos, the pain of people's lives, etc., that is, it is a reflection of the defects of the current social system, so its reasonable solution is after the entire social problem is solved, in other words, once the entire social problem is solved, this is fundamentally not a problem.

Why is this issue related to the entire social problem? The reason is this: The cause of venereal diseases is "prostitution." (Generally speaking) But why prostitute? Then there are two situations, one kind of person is full of food all day, idle and bored, and can not spend the time on business, proper entertainment, so "eating, drinking, prostitution, gambling" are all coming: another kind of person is because the age has reached or exceeded puberty, the need for sex has felt very urgent, but economically does not allow him to marry, or has a wife, but can not live together, to give reasonable satisfaction to sexual desire, so knowing that prostitution is dishonorable, is dangerous, also has to ignore everything, drink poison to quench thirst, take the risk to do this kind of thing. The former kind of person is not caused by sexual desire depression, although their nonsense is also due to environmental pressure, after all, they are not good themselves, so the editor does not think for them, the object discussed in this article is only the latter situation.

Now first say whether the frustration of sexual desire is a must for a person to satisfy because of sexual impulses. In the editor's opinion, this is not necessarily the case. Of course, sexual desire is human nature, and human beings must have it with considerable satisfaction, but the urgent desires or demands of people are not only sexual desire, just like the sentence "food and sex are also", but also have to be crowned with food, from which it can be seen that the requirement of sexual desire is not the whole of a person's requirements. Moreover, human desires are graded, and human beings must first satisfy the most important desires and then gradually extend to the important, secondary, etc. ["This is the explanation of the psychological school in economics for desire, and it is correct from a psychological point of view, but if it is applied to economics, it is wrong, but that is another matter, we do not need to pursue it. ) The proverb "When you are full and warm, you think of lust, when you are hungry and cold, you have the heart to steal" is also the same principle, so like our general poor masses, since we can not marry a wife because of the difficulty of life, we can not reasonably solve sexual desire, then it is better to put all his spirit and energy on improving the life and liberating the economy, etc. Moreover, in psychology, there is also the so-called transfer principle, that is, a person is forced in a certain aspect, can not make progress, he can put the spiritual effort to another aspect to seek development. The editor had such an experience when he was studying at the university, that is, all the male and female students who were ugly and economically not very affluent had to work harder and more diligently in their studies. Because they can not make a show of themselves in terms of appearance and economic conditions, they have to find another way out and find a way to show their faces. Therefore, although the editor does not ignore the importance of sexual desire like the general ascetics, he advocates that those who can not reasonably solve sexual desire should simply not solve it and do some effective work and things that can achieve the goal. It seems that this does not violate human nature, and may not be able to see it in practice!

Secondly, we will talk about the social reasons. Many people can not think of a way to improve or a way to struggle because of the蹇舛of their circumstances, the苦悶of their lives, and the窮困of their lives, so they simply ignore everything, embracing the attitude of 信陵君fine wine and women, and enjoying themselves to the fullest. Moreover, because of sexual impulses, absurd behaviors are mostly erotic pursuits. We see that Mr. Zhong Dai Er, who has personally experienced the pain of venereal diseases, attaches great importance to the pain of life and the hardships of the world, so we can know that the main cause of [prostitution] is not only [sexual desire], or even social reasons are the main cause, and [sexual desire] is just an誘質, because sexual desire is only the motive of [wanting to prostitute], and that kind of self-abandonment psychology is the resolution of [going to prostitute]. Therefore, we should pay great attention to this level: but this is generally speaking about society, saying that the prevalence of [prostitution] or [lascivious customs] in society, the spread of venereal diseases, is not [the world is not ancient] [people's hearts are greatly bad] but there are other objective reasons, it is possible, if individuals take this reason as a guise to forgive themselves, it is absolutely impossible. Because the bad social system and the pain of life are indeed the reasons for the degeneration of young people, but there is a way out in front of us, there is a fighting direction for us to get rid of these shackles, we not only do not need to be passive and颓废, but also passive and颓废, fundamentally is a kind of [slow killing, ] can never reduce the pain of the environment, but will increase it, so that you can not bear it (about passive and颓废, should be discussed separately, here do not say more) Therefore, young people who indulge in sensuality because of this, it is their own fault, which we can not tolerate.

In short, what the editor wants to tell the general youth in one sentence is: sexual impulses or frustrations are not harmful, only your own inability to cheer up is the main cause of making you step on the crisis.

Finally, the editor is deeply admired for the gentlemen who came to discuss the matter; they can sincerely tell the readers the pain they have felt, they can contribute methods with a spirit of service, all of which are rare spirits and attitudes in the current society. Editor

Novel

Rambling Tales of Siam (5)

— Yi Min

No Wife Without Being a Monk

In our country, being a monk is the most pitiful thing. Except for a few people who have seen through the mortal world and are willing to become monks themselves, most of them are sent to temples by their parents since they were young because of their poor family background, forcing him to spend those years without the joy of life, which does not seem very humane. Occasionally, one or two people can not stand the physiological pressure, and have to do some stealing chickens and dogs, and the society will责he does not abide by the rules, and even be subject to legal sanctions. But it is not the case in Siam: not only can monks have sons and daughters, but also have no qualifications to marry without being a monk. Therefore, none of the people in the country do not want to be a monk once, even if they are贵as kings, they have to shave their hair and live in the temple for a month or two. However, there are also many monks who are unwilling to return to俗. The reason for this is not that they despise情欲and discard尘缘. Originally Siam is a Buddhist country, and the status of monks is much higher than that of ordinary people. At the same time, the temples have huge temple properties, which can be used for them to squander. And although they do not marry wives, the problem of sex can still be solved semi-openly. Therefore, the Siamese monks who only consume but do not produce are also increasing day by day.

Every day at five or six o'clock in the morning, we can see monks wearing yellow robes and carrying iron bowls walking quickly, not looking at anything else, on any street, which is their daily alms collection.善男信女 see the monks coming, they hurry to run in front of him, and offer the prepared white rice, incense, coconut, or other foods with both hands. If the monk is willing to receive your offering with an iron bowl, you have to put your palms together and thank him. Even more strangely, every monk must have a young boy following him when he goes out, holding an umbrella for him in the sun and carrying a bag for him to buy things. It is really arrogant as凡! If you compare our country's monks with them, the 距离實在 is simply immeasurable.
